Dyadic Neo Enochian Magick

Complete Recipe Book

Copyright © 2026 Seth Thomas. All Rights Reserved.

Dyadic Neo Enochian Magick represents a fundamental departure from traditional magical practice. Where most systems rely on supplication to external entities, emotional intensity, or elaborate ritual to achieve results, this system operates as precision machinery. The practitioner does not petition; the practitioner engineers. By combining alchemical forces (Black/dissolution, White/purification, Green/growth, Red/manifestation) with elemental modes of operation (Air/mental, Water/emotional, Earth/material, Fire/active), specific transformations can be constructed with mechanical predictability. The power lies not in the fervor of your emotion or the favor of spirits, but in the structural relationships encoded within the working itself. This approach offers significant advantages: workings can be safely repeated without the drift that accompanies emotional transmutation, and every operation can be reversed with proper understanding—preserving practitioner sovereignty absolutely. The system presented here emerged from a single discovery about the mirror structure of the Enochian Great Table and has been developed through extensive practical application across domains of protection, finance, self-development, and love. Yet this Recipe Book represents early cartography of vast territory. The theoretical framework is robust and the configurations provided have been tested, but thousands of possible Subangle compositions remain unexplored, and the full implications of the system's fractal architecture continue to reveal themselves. What you hold is both a complete working system and an invitation to discovery.

This book provides everything needed to perform magical workings across four life domains. The opening tutorial (Parts I-V) teaches how to translate any dyadic configuration into a complete Enochian working with proper names and prayers. Parts VI and VII explain how to use the recipes and practical considerations. The recipe sections (Parts VIII-XI) offer pre-designed workings for common situations, each with configuration, charge, and reversal. Part XII combines workings into sequences for complex life situations. Part XIII and the Appendices provide quick reference and deeper theory.

Organization:

Parts I-V — Tutorial: Subangle grafting and prayer derivation
Part VI — How to use the recipes
Part VII — Practical considerations
Part VIII — Protection workings (29 configurations)
Part IX — Finance workings (20 configurations)
Part X — Self-Development workings (18 configurations)
Part XI — Love workings (23 configurations)
Part XII — Working sequences for common situations
Part XIII — Quick reference materials
Appendices — Detailed system mechanics

Before You Begin

This section provides the essential concepts you need before diving into the technical details. Read this first to understand what you're building and why it works.

The Core Discovery

The Enochian Great Table—that famous grid of letters received by John Dee in the 16th century—contains a hidden property that traditional interpretations missed entirely. The Table has a mirror structure: the same spatial arrangement (Red upper-left, White upper-right, Black lower-left, Green lower-right) appears at both the macro level (the four Watchtowers) and within each Watchtower (the four Subangles). This isn't decoration. It's functional architecture.

This mirror structure means that pieces from different Subangles can be combined—grafted together—while maintaining structural coherence. A column from the Black Subangle of the Red Watchtower can be placed into the White Subangle of the Green Watchtower, and the result still produces valid angel names with specific magical functions. The system you are learning exploits this property to construct transformations with precision.

Two Domains: What and How

Every working in this system operates through two independent domains:

The Alchemical Domain determines WHAT transforms—the quality and direction of change:

Black dissolves, clears, breaks down
White purifies, clarifies, stabilizes
Green grows, develops, expands
Red manifests, actualizes, completes

The Elemental Domain determines HOW that transformation propagates—the mode of operation:

Air works through thought, perception, communication
Water works through emotion, relationship, intuition
Earth works through structure, material conditions, physical reality
Fire works through action, will, direct force

A working that uses Black (dissolution) through Fire (action) operates very differently from Black through Water (emotion), even though both dissolve something. The first breaks things apart through decisive action; the second dissolves through emotional release or catharsis.

What Is a Dyad?

A dyad is simply a directional pair: one force providing context, another force emerging within that context.

When you see "White → Red," it means: within a context of White (purification, clarity), Red (manifestation) emerges. The first force (Outer/Macro) governs; the second force (Inner/Micro) acts. Think of it as a container and its contents, or a stage and the performance upon it.

Every working uses four dyads:

Host (H): The governing environment—where everything happens
Elemental (E): The mode of operation—how change propagates
Initial (I): The starting condition—what you're working with
Terminal (T): The end condition—what you're transforming it into

What Grafting Accomplishes

The grafting procedure physically combines columns from different Subangles around a Host structure. This isn't symbolic—it creates a specific arrangement of letters that produces specific angel names. Different combinations produce different names, and different names produce different effects.

When you select a configuration like "H: White→Red, E: Air→Fire, I: Black→White, T: White→Green," you are specifying exactly which Subangles contribute which pieces. The grafting procedure then shows you how to assemble them. The result is a complete working with fourteen angel names and a structured prayer.

What You Will Learn

Part I explains the system's architecture and the meaning of each component. Part II teaches the grafting procedure step by step. Part III shows how to derive all fourteen names from your grafted structure. Part IV gives you the prayer format. Part V walks through a complete example.

After completing Parts I-V, you will be able to take any configuration from the recipe sections (Parts VIII-XI) and translate it into a complete working—knowing exactly what each piece contributes and why the configuration produces its intended effect.

The recipes themselves are pre-designed configurations for common situations. You don't need to understand the full theory to use them effectively. But understanding the machinery gives you the ability to troubleshoot, modify, and eventually design your own workings for situations no recipe covers.

Let's begin.

Part I: Understanding the System

Before using the recipes, you must understand what each piece contributes to the working and how to locate the components within the Great Table.

1.1 The Spatial Arrangement

The Great Table is divided into four Watchtowers, and each Watchtower contains four Subangles. Both levels follow the same spatial arrangement:

In Both the Great Table and within each Watchtower:

Upper Left: Red
Upper Right: White
Lower Left: Black
Lower Right: Green

Within Each Subangle:

Calvary Cross Spine: Column 3
Calvary Cross Arms: Row 2
Kerubic Section: Row 1 excluding column 3
Servient Section: Rows 3-6 excluding column 3
Macro Servient Air Attribution: Row 3
Macro Servient Water Attribution: Row 4
Macro Servient Earth Attribution: Row 5
Macro Servient Fire Attribution: Row 6
Micro Servient Air Attribution: Column 1
Micro Servient Water Attribution: Column 2
Micro Servient Earth Attribution: Column 4
Micro Servient Fire Attribution: Column 5

Visual Reference

THE GREAT TABLE (Watchtower Arrangement) +---------------+---------------+ | | | | RED | WHITE | | (Upper Left) | (Upper Right) | | | | +---------------+---------------+ | | | | BLACK | GREEN | | (Lower Left) | (Lower Right) | | | | +---------------+---------------+ Each Watchtower contains four Subangles in the SAME arrangement: +-------+-------+ | Red | White | +-------+-------+ | Black | Green | +-------+-------+

This fractal pattern—the same arrangement at both levels—is fundamental to the system's architecture.

1.2 The Four Components of a Working

Every working in this system uses four dyads: Host (H), Elemental (E), Initial Graft (I), and Terminal Graft (T). Each serves a distinct function.

The Working Formula

A working has this structure:

I --> T (transformation) through E (method) within H (environment)

Or in plain language: "Something changes into something else, through a particular operational mode, within a governing context."

ANALOGY: Think of baking. The Initial Graft (I) is the raw ingredients. The Terminal Graft (T) is the finished dish. The Elemental (E) is the cooking method—baking, frying, steaming. The Host (H) is the kitchen environment—oven temperature, humidity, equipment. All four must work together for the transformation to succeed.

+--------------------------------------------------+ | HOST (H) | | Governing Environment | | | | INITIAL (I) ─────────────> TERMINAL (T) | | Starting via Achieved | | State ELEMENTAL (E) State | | Method of | | Propagation | +--------------------------------------------------+

The Host Dyad (H)

The Host provides the stable foundation and governing context for the entire working. It contributes the Calvary Cross (the spine and arms of the Subangle) to the newly grafted structure. Think of the Host as the container or environment in which the transformation occurs.

The Host determines:

  • The meta-environment governing the operation
  • Which Watchtower's hierarchy (God Names, King, Seniors, etc.) you invoke
  • The stable architecture around which the grafts are assembled

The Host does not change during the working. It is the constant context that holds and governs whatever transformation the grafts produce.

The Initial Graft (I)

The Initial Graft provides the starting point of the transformation. It contributes columns to the newly grafted Subangle based on where the first two letters of the Servient Angel are located. Think of the Initial Graft as "where you are coming from" or "what you are working with."

The Initial Graft determines:

  • The beginning state of the alchemical transformation
  • The material or condition being acted upon
  • The first half of the directional motion (I in the formula)

The Initial Graft represents the raw material, the problem, or the current state that the working will transform.

The Terminal Graft (T)

The Terminal Graft provides the end point of the transformation. It contributes columns to the newly grafted Subangle based on where the last two letters of the Servient Angel are located. Think of the Terminal Graft as "where you are going" or "what you are becoming."

The Terminal Graft determines:

  • The achieved state of the alchemical transformation
  • The goal or outcome being manifested
  • The second half of the directional motion (T in the formula)

The Terminal Graft represents the destination, the solution, or the transformed state that the working produces.

The Elemental Dyad (E)

The Elemental Dyad, realized through the Servient Angel, provides the operational mode and method of the working. It determines HOW the transformation propagates, not WHAT transforms. Think of the Elemental Dyad as the medium or channel through which the alchemical forces operate.

The Elemental Dyad determines:

  • The mode of operation (mental, emotional, structural, or active)
  • The method by which change manifests
  • Which specific Servient Angel carries the working

The Elemental Dyad remains constant throughout the operation. While the alchemical forces (Host and Grafts) may describe transformation, the Elemental Dyad describes the sustained style of that transformation.

1.3 Understanding Dyads

A dyad is written as Outer --> Inner (or equivalently, Inner within Outer).

Outer = the dominant CONTEXT, container, or governing force
Inner = the emerging INTENTION, content, or nascent force

Example: White --> Red means "within a purifying context (White), sovereignty (Red) is emerging."

Because each alchemical color and each element is itself a force-in-motion, a dyad represents a VECTOR - directional transformation with specific properties. Reversing the positions (Red --> White instead of White --> Red) creates a fundamentally different operation.

Terminology Note

Macro and Outer are interchangeable terms. Micro and Inner are interchangeable terms. When you see "White --> Red," the first color (White) is the Macro/Outer context, and the second color (Red) is the Micro/Inner emerging force.

DYAD NOTATION White --> Red | | | +-- Inner / Micro (emerging intention) +----------- Outer / Macro (governing context)

This notation appears throughout the book. "X to Y" and "X --> Y" mean the same thing: X is the Outer/Macro force, Y is the Inner/Micro force.

Locating Subangles by Alchemical Dyad

We locate a particular Subangle by its alchemical color dyad, which gives the location within the Great Table:

Macro Red, Micro Red: Upper Left Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Red, Micro White: Upper Left Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Red, Micro Black: Upper Left Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Red, Micro Green: Upper Left Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro White, Micro Red: Upper Right Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro White, Micro White: Upper Right Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro White, Micro Black: Upper Right Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro White, Micro Green: Upper Right Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro Black, Micro Red: Lower Left Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Black, Micro White: Lower Left Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Black, Micro Black: Lower Left Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Black, Micro Green: Lower Left Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro Green, Micro Red: Lower Right Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Green, Micro White: Lower Right Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Green, Micro Black: Lower Right Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Green, Micro Green: Lower Right Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Locating Servient Angels by Elemental Dyad

We locate a particular Servient Angel by its elemental dyad, which gives the location within the Subangle (the coordinate of the first letter):

Macro Air, Micro Air (Air to Air): Row 3, Column 1
Macro Air, Micro Water (Air to Water): Row 3, Column 2
Macro Air, Micro Earth (Air to Earth): Row 3, Column 4
Macro Air, Micro Fire (Air to Fire): Row 3, Column 5

Macro Water, Micro Air (Water to Air): Row 4, Column 1
Macro Water, Micro Water (Water to Water): Row 4, Column 2
Macro Water, Micro Earth (Water to Earth): Row 4, Column 4
Macro Water, Micro Fire (Water to Fire): Row 4, Column 5

Macro Earth, Micro Air (Earth to Air): Row 5, Column 1
Macro Earth, Micro Water (Earth to Water): Row 5, Column 2
Macro Earth, Micro Earth (Earth to Earth): Row 5, Column 4
Macro Earth, Micro Fire (Earth to Fire): Row 5, Column 5

Macro Fire, Micro Air (Fire to Air): Row 6, Column 1
Macro Fire, Micro Water (Fire to Water): Row 6, Column 2
Macro Fire, Micro Earth (Fire to Earth): Row 6, Column 4
Macro Fire, Micro Fire (Fire to Fire): Row 6, Column 5

1.4 The Alchemical Colors

The four alchemical colors represent phases of transformation. Each is a force-in-motion, not a static quality.

Red in the Macro (Watchtower) Context

Red at the Watchtower level governs workings of embodiment, sovereignty, and manifestation. When Red is the Macro color, the entire working operates within a context of claiming authority, establishing presence, and bringing things into full expression. Red Watchtower workings tend toward assertive, commanding operations where the practitioner exercises sovereign will.

Use Red Macro for: Establishing authority, claiming territory, manifesting intentions, completing processes, exercising sovereignty, taking command.

Black in the Macro (Watchtower) Context

Black at the Watchtower level governs workings of dissolution, breakdown, and shadow confrontation. When Black is the Macro color, the entire working operates within a context of entropy, clearing, and reducing to fundamentals. Black Watchtower workings tend toward operations that break down existing structures, reveal hidden foundations, or clear away what no longer serves.

Use Black Macro for: Dissolving obstacles, breaking patterns, shadow work, clearing accumulated debris, stripping away illusions, returning to basics.

White in the Macro (Watchtower) Context

White at the Watchtower level governs workings of purification, refinement, and clarification. When White is the Macro color, the entire working operates within a context of cleansing, distillation, and increasing coherence. White Watchtower workings tend toward operations that remove impurities, bring clarity, and separate essence from dross.

Use White Macro for: Purification, cleansing, gaining clarity, refining processes, filtering influences, achieving precision, distilling essence.

Green in the Macro (Watchtower) Context

Green at the Watchtower level governs workings of growth, generation, and organic expansion. When Green is the Macro color, the entire working operates within a context of proliferation, connection, and vital development. Green Watchtower workings tend toward operations that create, multiply, network, and foster living systems.

Use Green Macro for: Growth, creation, expansion, networking, fertility, nurturing development, building connections, fostering abundance.

Red in the Micro (Subangle) Context

Red at the Subangle level specifies the emerging intention within the broader Watchtower context. As the Micro color, Red represents sovereignty, authority, or manifestation that is crystallizing within whatever larger context governs. Red Micro adds a quality of completion, claiming, or embodiment to the working.

Use Red Micro for: Adding sovereign completion, manifesting within a process, claiming authority within a context, bringing something to full expression.

Black in the Micro (Subangle) Context

Black at the Subangle level specifies dissolution or breakdown as the emerging intention. As the Micro color, Black represents entropy, clearing, or shadow exposure crystallizing within the broader context. Black Micro adds a quality of breaking down, revealing foundations, or confronting shadow.

Use Black Micro for: Adding dissolution within a process, breaking down specific elements, revealing hidden aspects, clearing within a larger context.

White in the Micro (Subangle) Context

White at the Subangle level specifies purification or refinement as the emerging intention. As the Micro color, White represents cleansing, clarity, or distillation crystallizing within the broader context. White Micro adds a quality of purifying, clarifying, or filtering specific elements.

Use White Micro for: Adding purification within a process, clarifying specific aspects, filtering particular influences, refining within context.

Green in the Micro (Subangle) Context

Green at the Subangle level specifies growth or generation as the emerging intention. As the Micro color, Green represents proliferation, connection, or organic development crystallizing within the broader context. Green Micro adds a quality of growing, expanding, or nurturing specific elements.

Use Green Micro for: Adding growth within a process, expanding specific aspects, creating connections, nurturing development within a larger context.

1.5 The Elemental Modes

The four elements describe HOW change propagates, not WHAT changes. They are the operational method through which alchemical forces manifest.

Air in the Macro (Row) Context

Air as the Macro element means the operation primarily moves through the mental realm - through thought, communication, understanding, and strategy. Air Macro operations work by changing how things are conceived, planned, communicated, or understood. The working propagates through ideas and words.

Use Air Macro for: Mental operations, communication work, strategic planning, intellectual development, clarity-seeking, establishing mental boundaries.

Water in the Macro (Row) Context

Water as the Macro element means the operation primarily moves through the emotional realm - through feeling, intuition, receptivity, and flow. Water Macro operations work by changing how things are felt, sensed, or emotionally processed. The working propagates through empathy and adaptation.

Use Water Macro for: Emotional processing, relationship work, intuitive development, adaptive responses, flow states, establishing emotional boundaries.

Earth in the Macro (Row) Context

Earth as the Macro element means the operation primarily moves through the structural realm - through building, anchoring, materializing, and stabilizing. Earth Macro operations work by changing tangible structures, physical reality, or stable foundations. The working propagates through solid manifestation.

Use Earth Macro for: Manifestation work, building tangible things, grounding operations, structural establishment, material world engagement, physical boundaries.

Fire in the Macro (Row) Context

Fire as the Macro element means the operation primarily moves through the active realm - through will, direct action, transformation, and intensity. Fire Macro operations work by forcing change through energetic intervention. The working propagates through dynamic force and catalytic action.

Use Fire Macro for: Crisis intervention, rapid change, willful transformation, dynamic action, catalytic work, establishing energetic boundaries.

Air in the Micro (Column) Context

Air as the Micro element specifies the emerging operational mode within the broader elemental context. Air Micro adds mental clarity, communicative precision, or strategic thinking to whatever primary mode governs the working.

Use Air Micro for: Adding mental precision, clarifying communication, strategic refinement within the primary operational mode.

Water in the Micro (Column) Context

Water as the Micro element specifies emotional flow or intuitive sensitivity emerging within the broader operational context. Water Micro adds empathic responsiveness, adaptive flexibility, or emotional depth to the working.

Use Water Micro for: Adding emotional sensitivity, intuitive guidance, adaptive flexibility within the primary operational mode.

Earth in the Micro (Column) Context

Earth as the Micro element specifies grounding or structural anchoring emerging within the broader operational context. Earth Micro adds stability, tangible results, or practical manifestation to the working.

Use Earth Micro for: Adding structural stability, grounding results, practical anchoring within the primary operational mode.

Fire in the Micro (Column) Context

Fire as the Micro element specifies dynamic action or willful force emerging within the broader operational context. Fire Micro adds urgency, intensity, or catalytic transformation to the working.

Use Fire Micro for: Adding dynamic force, urgent action, catalytic intensity within the primary operational mode.

The Translation Between Domains

The elemental domain and the alchemical domain correspond through a precise translation:

Red (alchemical) ↔ Air (elemental) Black (alchemical) ↔ Water (elemental) White (alchemical) ↔ Earth (elemental) Green (alchemical) ↔ Fire (elemental)

This translation preserves class structure: a Class +1 alchemical dyad translates to a Class +1 elemental dyad. For example, Black --> White (alchemical Class +1) corresponds to Water --> Earth (elemental Class +1).

This matters for resonance assessment—when your elemental dyad matches or harmonizes with your alchemical configuration, effects can be amplified. Appendix C explores resonance in full detail.

1.6 Configuration Types: A Preview

Configuration types (I through V) describe the relationship between Host and Graft dyads. This relationship determines how long your working persists and whether it maintains itself:

Type I: All three differ (H ≠ I ≠ T) — Flexible, fades naturally Type II: Host matches start (H = I) — Momentum from established base Type III: Host matches end (H = T) — Achieved state becomes self-maintaining Type IV: All three match (H = I = T) — Absolute permanence, resists all change Type V: Grafts match, host differs (I = T ≠ H) — Maintained constancy under pressure

You will select configuration type based on how long you need the effect to persist and whether it should maintain itself. Part VI and Appendix A explain configuration types in full detail. For now, simply know that the recipes specify configuration type for good reasons—the type is not arbitrary but matches the working's purpose.

1.7 Class Structure: A Preview

Every dyad belongs to one of four classes based on the relationship between its Outer and Inner components. Class tells you about the intensity and character of the dyad's motion.

Class 0: Identity

Inner = Outer (same force on both sides)

Alchemical examples: Black --> Black, White --> White, Green --> Green, Red --> Red
Elemental examples: Air --> Air, Water --> Water, Earth --> Earth, Fire --> Fire

Property: Self-reinforcing stasis, maximum intensity of one quality, no internal motion.

Use for: Seals, wards, anchoring, maximum fixation.

Class +1: Progressive

Inner is one step forward in the natural sequence.

Alchemical examples: Black --> White, White --> Green, Green --> Red, Red --> Black
Elemental examples: Air --> Water, Water --> Earth, Earth --> Fire, Fire --> Air

Property: Developmental flow, organic progression, natural next step.

Use for: Gradual change, learning, skill building, gentle development.

Class -1: Regressive

Inner is one step backward in the natural sequence.

Alchemical examples: White --> Black, Green --> White, Red --> Green, Black --> Red
Elemental examples: Water --> Air, Earth --> Water, Fire --> Earth, Air --> Fire

Property: Corrective motion, return, grounding, conservation.

Use for: Error correction, integration, returning to fundamentals.

Class ±2: Opposition

Inner skips to the opposite side.

Alchemical examples: Black --> Green, White --> Red, Green --> Black, Red --> White
Elemental examples: Air --> Earth, Water --> Fire, Earth --> Air, Fire --> Water

Property: Dialectical tension, skip-level bridging, productive paradox.

Use for: Breakthrough workings, integrating opposites, quantum leaps.

When reading recipes, you will see class assignments like "H: White to Red (Class ±2)". This tells you the dyad bridges opposites—it's a breakthrough-level force, not a gentle developmental one. Appendix B provides the complete class reference.

Part II: The Grafting Procedure

This section provides step-by-step instructions for assembling a grafted Subangle from your chosen configuration.

2.1 Understand Your Configuration

Before grafting, identify the four dyads from your chosen recipe:

H (Host): The alchemical dyad providing the Calvary Cross
E (Elemental): The elemental dyad selecting the Servient Angel
I (Initial Graft): The alchemical dyad providing the first graft columns
T (Terminal Graft): The alchemical dyad providing the final graft columns

2.2 Locate the Host Subangle

Using the Host dyad, find the Subangle that will provide the Calvary Cross:

Macro Red, Micro Red: Upper Left Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Red, Micro White: Upper Left Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Red, Micro Black: Upper Left Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Red, Micro Green: Upper Left Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro White, Micro Red: Upper Right Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro White, Micro White: Upper Right Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro White, Micro Black: Upper Right Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro White, Micro Green: Upper Right Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro Black, Micro Red: Lower Left Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Black, Micro White: Lower Left Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Black, Micro Black: Lower Left Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Black, Micro Green: Lower Left Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

Macro Green, Micro Red: Lower Right Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle
Macro Green, Micro White: Lower Right Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle
Macro Green, Micro Black: Lower Right Watchtower, Lower Left Subangle
Macro Green, Micro Green: Lower Right Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

2.3 Determine the Servient Angel Location

Using the Elemental dyad, find the generic location of the first letter of the Servient Angel you will use:

Air to Air: Row 3, Column 1
Air to Water: Row 3, Column 2
Air to Earth: Row 3, Column 4
Air to Fire: Row 3, Column 5

Water to Air: Row 4, Column 1
Water to Water: Row 4, Column 2
Water to Earth: Row 4, Column 4
Water to Fire: Row 4, Column 5

Earth to Air: Row 5, Column 1
Earth to Water: Row 5, Column 2
Earth to Earth: Row 5, Column 4
Earth to Fire: Row 5, Column 5

Fire to Air: Row 6, Column 1
Fire to Water: Row 6, Column 2
Fire to Earth: Row 6, Column 4
Fire to Fire: Row 6, Column 5

2.4 Locate the Initial Graft Subangle and Extract Columns

After locating the Initial Graft Subangle within the Great Table using the Initial Dyad, from that Subangle take the columns containing the first two letters of the chosen Servient Angel. Include rows 1, 3, 4, 5, 6 (skip row 2, which is the Calvary Cross arm).

The columns to extract depend on the Micro elemental attribution:

Micro Air: Columns 1 and 2
Micro Water: Columns 2 and 4
Micro Earth: Columns 4 and 5
Micro Fire: Columns 5 and 1

2.5 Place the Initial Graft Columns

Place the extracted columns in the same positions around the Host Subangle's Calvary Cross. The columns go in the same locations they came from.

2.6 Locate the Terminal Graft Subangle and Extract Columns

After locating the Terminal Graft Subangle within the Great Table using the Terminal Dyad, from that Subangle, take the columns containing the last two letters of the chosen Servient Angel. Include rows 1, 3, 4, 5, 6.

The columns to extract depend on the Micro elemental attribution:

Micro Air: Columns 4 and 5
Micro Water: Columns 5 and 1
Micro Earth: Columns 1 and 2
Micro Fire: Columns 2 and 4

2.7 Place the Terminal Graft Columns

Place the extracted columns in the same positions around the Host Subangle's Calvary Cross, completing the grafted Subangle.

2.8 Add the Prefixes

The prefixes come from the Tablet of Union. They are positioned:

  • Vertically to the left of the Subangle (beside rows 1, 3, 4, 5, 6)
  • Horizontally above the Subangle (above columns 1, 2, 4, 5)

The prefixes are determined by the HOST dyad:

Macro Prefixes (Vertical, from the Host's Watchtower):

Macro Red: a, e, x, r, p
Macro White: o, h, C, m, a
Macro Black: n, n, a, T, a
Macro Green: t, b, i, o, m

Micro Prefixes (Horizontal, from the Host's Subangle position):

Micro Red: e, h, n, b
Micro White: x, C, a, i
Micro Black: r, m, T, o
Micro Green: p, a, a, m

Now you have a complete grafted Subangle.

3.3 Subangle Names

These names must be derived from your specific grafted Subangle. The formulas below tell you where to find each letter.

Prince (5 letters):

Letter 1: Row 2, Column 2
Letter 2: Row 1, Column 3
Letter 3: Row 2, Column 4
Letter 4: Row 3, Column 3
Letter 5: Row 2, Column 3

Summoning Angel (6 letters): Column 3, reading down (rows 1-6)

Commanding Angel (5 letters): Row 2, reading across (columns 1-5)

Kerubic Angel (4 letters): Start at Row 1 in the same column as the first letter of your Servient Angel. Follow Row 1 to the right, skipping Column 3, wrapping from Column 5 back to Column 1, until you have 4 letters.

Ruling Angel (5 letters):

Letter 1: Row 1, same column as first letter of Servient Angel
Letter 2: First letter of the Servient Angel itself
Letters 3-5: Follow down from the Servient Angel's first letter, wrapping from Row 6 back to Row 3, until you have 5 letters total

Servient Angel (4 letters): Start at the coordinate of your chosen Elemental Dyad (see Step 3). Follow the row to the right, skipping Column 3, wrapping from Column 5 to Column 1, until you have 4 letters.

Archangelic Kerubic Angel (5 letters): Add the vertical prefix letter for Row 1 to the beginning of the Kerubic Angel's name.

Archangelic Ruling Angel (6 letters): Add the horizontal prefix letter above the Ruling Angel's column to the beginning of the Ruling Angel's name.

Archangelic Servient Angel (5 letters): Add the vertical prefix letter for the Servient Angel's row to the beginning of the Servient Angel's name.

Mercurial Kerubic Angel (5 letters): Insert the letter at Row 1, Column 3 as the third letter of the Kerubic Angel's name, shifting the last two letters right.

Mercurial Ruling Angel (6 letters): Insert the letter at Row 2 in the same column as the Ruling Angel's first letter as the second letter, shifting the last four letters right.

Mercurial Servient Angel (5 letters): Insert the letter at Column 3 on the same row as the Servient Angel as the third letter, shifting the last two letters right.

Kerubic Regent Cacodaemon (3 letters): The same prefix as the Archangelic Kerubic Angel plus the first two letters of the Kerubic Angel's name.

Kerubic Rooted Cacodaemon (3 letters): The same prefix as the Archangelic Kerubic Angel plus the last two letters of the Kerubic Angel's name.

Servient Regent Cacodaemon (3 letters): The same prefix as the Archangelic Servient Angel plus the first two letters of the Servient Angel's name.

Servient Rooted Cacodaemon (3 letters): The same prefix as the Archangelic Servient Angel plus the last two letters of the Servient Angel's name.

Part V: Your First Working

This walkthrough takes you through a complete working from recipe to prayer. We'll use recipe 8.1.1b—Self-Cleansing (Type I)—because it's simple, immediately useful, and demonstrates all the essential procedures.

5.1 Why This Recipe

Self-Cleansing (Type I) is ideal for your first working because:

  • Type I workings complete and release naturally—no reversal needed
  • The use case is universal: everyone accumulates energetic residue
  • All four dyads are Class +1 (gentle, progressive motion)
  • The configuration produces clear, predictable results

If anything feels unclear as you work through this, you can always perform the working and then return to study the mechanics later.

5.2 The Recipe

From Part VIII (Protection Recipes), recipe 8.1.1b:

Use Case

When clearing FOR a specific purpose rather than establishing ongoing purity. Use before ritual work, after a particular difficult encounter, or as preparation for what comes next. Appropriate when you need to be clean NOW but do not require permanent purification—the cleansing completes and releases.

Working Configuration

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to White (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible purification that completes and releases; cleansing for this moment.

Charge

All that is not mine dissolves—now, for this purpose, in this moment. I clear the residue of what I have encountered and return to myself, clean enough for what comes next. This purification completes itself and asks nothing further. I am cleansed. The work is done. Normal life resumes.

5.3 Understand What Each Dyad Does

Before grafting, understand what each component contributes:

H: White to Green (Host)
The environmental container for the working. White provides purified sovereignty; Green provides fertile emergence. The working operates within a context of "pure ground supporting new growth."

E: Water to Earth (Elemental)
HOW the transformation manifests. Water is emotional/flowing; Earth is structural/material. The cleansing works by "emotional flow grounding into stable structure"—feelings become settled reality.

I: Black to White (Initial Graft)
WHERE the transformation starts. Black is dissolution; White is purification. The starting point is "dissolution being purified"—whatever accumulated debris exists is being refined away.

T: Green to Red (Terminal Graft)
WHERE the transformation ends. Green is growth; Red is manifestation. The endpoint is "growth manifesting actively"—new clean energy emerging into expression.

The full arc: Within a purifying environment (H), through emotional grounding (E), dissolution-becoming-pure (I) transforms into growth-becoming-manifest (T). You start contaminated; you end clean and active.

5.4 Locate the Subangles

Using the mappings from Part I (section 1.1), find each Subangle:

H: White to Green
Macro White = Upper Right Watchtower
Micro Green = Lower Right Subangle
Location: Upper Right Watchtower, Lower Right Subangle

I: Black to White
Macro Black = Lower Left Watchtower
Micro White = Upper Right Subangle
Location: Lower Left Watchtower, Upper Right Subangle

T: Green to Red
Macro Green = Lower Right Watchtower
Micro Red = Upper Left Subangle
Location: Lower Right Watchtower, Upper Left Subangle

5.5 Determine Which Columns to Graft

The Elemental dyad E: Water to Earth has Micro Earth. From the grafting rules:

Micro Earth: Initial Graft contributes Columns 4 and 5
Micro Earth: Terminal Graft contributes Columns 1 and 2

So from Black to White, you take Columns 4 and 5.
From Green to Red, you take Columns 1 and 2.

5.6 Locate the Servient Angel Position

The Elemental dyad also determines the Servient Angel's first letter:

Water to Earth: Row 4, Column 4

This position is marked with * in the grafted Subangle and determines which angels you derive.

Servient Rooted Cacodaemon: Cab (prefix C + last 2 of alab: ab)

5.11 Assemble the Prayer

LUAH - ZIR MOZ IAD - ZIR ZOD IAM - AH OH NEH TAH LANG - ZNA BAB IAD - BNA ZAD IAB - NEH TEH AH OH URCH - GRV SOR IAD - RRV GOD IAS - OH NEH TEH AH SACH - OSF SER IAD - RSF OED IAS - TEH AH OH NAH Ol vinu od zacam, ils gah oRado Raido Rado oRa odo Od ils gah Calab alaab alab Cal Cab Od lansh vors gi iad, gohus pugo ils miiso od darbs! Dooiop ONTA MTOR MAOHC Od Dooiop mph arsl gaich Od Dooiap raagios lsrahpm saiinov lavazrp slgaich ligdisa soaiznt Od Dooiap raagiol Tipaa Od Dooiap iaaasd aTapa Od Dooiap oRado aRamhg Calab Od Dooiap Raido Rpamhg alaab Od Dooiap Rado Ramhg alab Od Dooiap oRa odo Cal Cab Ol vinu od zacam, ils gah oRado Raido Rado oRa odo Od ils gah Calab alaab alab Cal Cab [DELIVER YOUR CHARGE HERE]

5.12 Deliver the Charge

After completing the prayer, deliver the charge with clear intention:

"All that is not mine dissolves—now, for this purpose, in this moment. I clear the residue of what I have encountered and return to myself, clean enough for what comes next. This purification completes itself and asks nothing further. I am cleansed. The work is done. Normal life resumes."

Speak it aloud with conviction. The prayer has assembled the machinery; the charge tells it what to do.

5.13 What Happens Next

Type I workings complete and release naturally. You may feel an immediate shift, or the cleansing may work gradually over hours or days. The working will fade on its own—no reversal required unless you specifically want to close the cycle early.

You have now completed your first working.

If you want to understand the grafting procedure in more technical detail, see Part II. If you're ready to select recipes for your own purposes, skip to Part VI.

Part VI: How to Use the Recipes

This section explains how to read the recipes, understand the alternatives provided, and select the configuration type that matches your situation.

6.1 Recipe Structure

Each recipe follows a standard format:

TITLE AND SUBTITLE — The name and brief description of the operation.

USE CASE — When to use this working. Read carefully—the USE CASE describes the specific situation this configuration serves. If your situation differs significantly, a different recipe or configuration type may serve better.

WORKING CONFIGURATION — The four dyads (H, E, I, T) with their class assignments and the configuration type. This is what you bring to the grafting procedure.

H: Host (Alchemical) - The environmental force E: Elemental - The operational mode I: Initial Graft (Alchemical) - Where the transformation begins T: Terminal Graft (Alchemical) - Where the transformation completes

FUNCTION — What the working does mechanically—how the forces interact to produce the intended effect.

CHARGE — The spoken declaration that focuses intent and delivers the working. Use as written, or adapt to your own voice while preserving the core elements.

REVERSAL CONFIGURATION — Every working includes a reversal. This is the configuration to undo or release the primary working when it has served its purpose or if circumstances change. Never deploy a working without understanding how to reverse it.

6.2 Understanding Alternatives

Many recipes include alternatives, marked with letter suffixes (a, b, c). These are NOT interchangeable—each serves a different situation.

PRIMARY RECIPES (usually "a") — The main configuration, typically designed for lasting or self-maintaining effect. Use when you want the working to persist and maintain itself over time.

ALTERNATIVE RECIPES (usually "b" or "c") — Different configuration types serving the same general purpose but with different temporal and mechanical properties. Read each USE CASE carefully to determine which matches your actual situation.

Example:

8.1.1a Self-Cleansing (Type III - Lasting Purity) — For establishing ongoing, self-maintaining purification. The cleansed state locks into place and maintains itself.

8.1.1b Self-Cleansing (Type I - Temporary Cleansing) — For clearing before a specific event or after a particular encounter. The cleansing completes and naturally releases—it does not persist.

The same operation—cleansing—but with fundamentally different temporal properties. Choose based on what you actually need.

6.3 Configuration Types: When to Use Each

The five configuration types produce fundamentally different mechanical behavior. Your choice of type determines how the working functions, how long it persists, and how difficult it is to reverse.

Type I: Linear Transition

Structure: H differs from I differs from T
Properties: Maximum flexibility, does not self-maintain

WHEN TO USE:

• Exploratory work, learning arcs, broad transformations
• Temporary operations with defined duration
• When you want the effect to naturally release when complete
• Situations requiring flexibility rather than permanence
• Preparation for specific events or windows of activity

REVERSAL: Easiest. Often fades naturally when no longer reinforced.

Type II: Origin Reinforcement

Structure: H = I, both differ from T
Properties: Momentum from established base, moderate persistence

WHEN TO USE:

• Building on existing strengths or authority
• Expanding from a stable foundation
• When the starting point is already part of your environment
• Developmental work that extends what you already have
• Launching from secure position toward new territory

REVERSAL: Moderate. Establish new origin or allow gradual decay.

Type III: Destination Locking

Structure: H = T, both differ from I
Properties: Achieved state becomes self-maintaining, high persistence

WHEN TO USE:

• Sovereignty installation and protection workings
• Identity-level shifts that should persist
• Creating self-maintaining boundaries
• When the achieved state should become "the new normal"
• Situations where you want reality to enforce the change

SUBTYPE — MIRROR INVERSION (I and T are reversals of each other):

• Creates self-correcting systems
• Both grafts must be Class ±2
• Excellent for dynamic protection that responds to violations

REVERSAL: Difficult. Requires active dismantling—decay is insufficient.

Type IV: Absolute Identity

Structure: H = I = T
Properties: Total fixation, no motion permitted, maximum permanence

WHEN TO USE:

• Seals, wards, vows, permanent patterns
• When change itself must be prevented
• Locking something in place forever (or until deliberately broken)
• Situations requiring absolute constancy

CAUTION: Use deliberately. Type IV creates conditions that resist all change, including beneficial adaptation. Appropriate for sealing and permanent boundaries, but excessive use creates rigidity.

REVERSAL: Most difficult. Requires external force to break total fixation.

Type V: Parallel Reinforcement

Structure: H differs from I = T
Properties: Maintained constancy under opposing pressure

WHEN TO USE:

• Holding a state against environmental opposition
• Integrity work under pressure
• When you need to maintain something despite contrary forces
• Forge-tempering: resistance creates resilience
• Situations where the environment pushes against your intent

REVERSAL: Moderate. Removing opposition pressure often sufficient.

6.4 Selection Principles

Match Configuration to Intent

Temporary need → Type I (flexibility, natural release) Building on strength → Type II (momentum from base) Lasting change → Type III (destination locking) Permanent seal → Type IV (absolute fixation) Holding under pressure → Type V (maintained constancy)

Match Intensity to Situation

Mild intervention → Class +1, progressive elementals Moderate transformation → Class ±2 Host with Class +1 grafts Breakthrough work → Class ±2 throughout, dialectical elementals

Do Not Default

There is no "safe default." A Type I working applied to a sovereignty need will fail to hold. A Type IV working applied to developmental need will create harmful rigidity. Match configuration to actual intent.

Read Use Cases Carefully

The USE CASE descriptions distinguish between alternatives. If your situation matches the Type I alternative better than the Type III primary, use the Type I. Configuration type is not a hierarchy—it is a taxonomy of different mechanical behaviors.

Important Note on Multiple Workings

Before selecting your first recipe, understand this: deploy one working at a time. Wait at least a few days to a week before adding another. Multiple simultaneous workings can create interference or contradictory effects. Even complementary workings benefit from spacing—let each one begin manifesting before adding the next. Section 7.5 discusses layering in more detail.

6.5 Reversals and Safety

Every working in this book includes a reversal configuration. This is not optional material—it is essential to practitioner sovereignty.

PRINCIPLES:

1. Never deploy a working without understanding how to reverse it
2. Document what you deploy so you can reverse it later if needed
3. Type III and IV reversals require active work—they do not decay
4. Keep reversal configurations accessible for any ongoing working

The reversal USE CASE describes when to reverse. The reversal CHARGE provides the language for releasing. The reversal CONFIGURATION gives you the dyads to construct the reversal working through the same grafting procedure.

Part VII: Practical Considerations

This section addresses common questions about working with the system in practice: timing, tracking, setup, pronunciation, and working with multiple operations.

7.1 Timing

This system is timing-agnostic. There are no required moon phases, planetary hours, or days of the week. The machinery works when you work it.

Results typically begin manifesting within days, but timing varies based on your circumstances. Magick operates by nudging odds and creating opportunities. What you have access to and your degrees of freedom highly influence how quickly effects appear. A working for financial opportunity manifests differently for someone actively networking than for someone in isolation.

If you wish to coordinate with planetary magick, astrological timing, or other systems, the machinery accommodates this. Such coordination can bolster your work but is not necessary for effectiveness.

7.2 Tracking Results

Pay attention. Keep notes.

The system does not announce when workings are active, fading, or complete. You must observe your own life and notice what shifts. A working for protection may manifest as avoided conflicts, changed circumstances, or subtle redirections you only recognize in retrospect.

Recommended practice:

• Record what you deploy: configuration, date, charge, purpose
• Note when effects appear and how they manifest
• Track when workings seem to fade or complete their purpose
• Document reversals when performed

You are your own best diagnostic tool. The more attention you pay, the more clearly you will understand how the system operates in your life.

7.3 Ritual Setup

Minimal requirements:

At best: The Great Table (Tabula Recensa) within sight
At least: The grafted Subangle in front of you

Beyond this, the system flexes to accommodate whatever symbolic framing helps you focus. Candles, incense, planetary correspondences, specific postures, dedicated space—all of these can help you enter the right headspace for clear intention, but none are mechanically required.

The power is in the names and the prayer. Everything else is support for your concentration and seriousness of purpose.

7.4 Pronunciation

One of the unique aspects of Enochian is that it was channeled by Dee and Kelley in English, so the pronunciation, for the most part, follows English rules.

• Add "uh," "eh," or "ah" between consonants. Use whichever sounds best to you.
• Add a slight pause between repeated letters: aala would be AH-AH-LA, for instance.
• Add an "uh," "eh," or "ah" after capital letters: aROo would be AH-RAH-OH-OH.

Speak with intention and clarity. The names carry the encoding; your voice activates them.

7.5 Layering Workings

Spread them out. Let them breathe.

Each working is designed with your CURRENT state in mind. It then moves you to an entirely different state. Firing many workings at once risks pulling yourself in contradictory directions before any single working has begun to manifest.

Recommended practice:

• Deploy one working
• Give it time to begin manifesting (typically a few days to a week)
• Observe what shifts
• Then consider whether additional workings are needed

This is theory based on the mechanical properties of the system. Experiments must be conducted. But caution suggests allowing each working space to operate before layering additional forces.

If you do run multiple workings simultaneously, ensure they are complementary rather than contradictory. Protection and finance workings may coexist well. Two different protection workings with conflicting approaches may create interference.

7.6 Working for Others

Workings for others are possible but appear to be less potent than workings for yourself. The system seems optimized for self-directed operation—you are the Operator providing Divine Intent and Compelling Will, and your own transformation is the most direct application.

When working for others:

• Ensure you have their consent
• Adapt the charge to reference them specifically
• Recognize that results may be less pronounced than self-work
• Consider teaching them to work the system themselves

Experimentation is encouraged. The boundaries of the system are discovered through practice.

7.8 The Tablet of Union

The Tablet of Union provides the Archangelic prefixes and the three Archangels called in the prayer. It sits at the center of the Great Table and serves as the Operator's interface to the entire system.

When Spirit is placed in the center column (AONT), the Tablet of Union mirrors the elemental structure of the Servient Section:

Row 1: Air       Column 1: Air
Row 2: Water     Column 2: Water
Row 3: Earth     Column 3: Spirit
Row 4: Fire      Column 4: Earth
                 Column 5: Fire

|---+---+---+---+---|
| b | i | t | o | m |

Part VIII: Protection Recipes

Dyadic configurations and charges for protection and boundary work. Organized from innermost personal work to outermost boundary operations.

8.1 Self-Restoration

Operations focused on healing, cleansing, and reclaiming your own energy.

8.1.1a Self-Cleansing

Internal purification within protected space

Use Case

When you feel contaminated by foreign energies, carrying residue from difficult interactions, or need to clear accumulated psychic debris. Use after exposure to hostile environments, draining people, or chaotic situations. Appropriate when you feel "not yourself" or weighed down by what isn't yours.

Working Configuration

H: White to Red (Class +/-2) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to White (Class +1) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type III (Destination Locking) Purified sovereignty becomes self-maintaining; cleansing completes into wholeness. RATIONALE: Type III locks purity as the new environmental law. Without destination locking, you would need to repeatedly cleanse; Type III makes the purified state self-sustaining.

Function

Dissolves all foreign energies, residues, and accumulations within your being, leaving only what is authentically yours. The purified state locks into place and maintains itself without ongoing effort.

Charge

All that is not mine dissolves into nothing. Every foreign thread, every borrowed weight, every residue of what was never truly me--gone. What remains is clarified, settled, and wholly my own. I am the still water that knows only its own depth. Purity maintains itself here, effortlessly and completely.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the cleansing is complete and you're ready to resume normal life. Use when prolonged purification has left you too isolated, too sterile, or cut off from beneficial exchange. Appropriate when the protective intensity is no longer needed and you want to re-engage with the world.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Fire to Water (Class +/-2) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: White to Black (Class -1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible dissolution of the cleansing field under generative governance. RATIONALE: Type I allows gentle release without creating a new locked state. The reversal completes and fades, returning you to normal permeability rather than locking in a new pattern.

Function

Releases the self-maintaining purification field, allowing normal energetic exchange and accumulation to resume. The intense cleansing cycle completes, and you return to ordinary permeability.

Reversal Charge

The purifying flame softens to living warmth. I welcome the dust of the world upon me once more, for I am strong enough to carry it. The crystalline stillness melts into flowing life. I release the need for absolute purity and embrace the beautiful mess of existence. The cleansing is complete--I return to the rhythm of ordinary accumulation.

8.1.1b Self-Cleansing - Type I Alternative

Temporary Cleansing

Use Case

When clearing FOR a specific purpose rather than establishing ongoing purity. Use before ritual work, after a particular difficult encounter, or as preparation for what comes next. Appropriate when you need to be clean NOW but do not require permanent purification--the cleansing completes and releases.

Working Configuration

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to White (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible purification that completes and releases; cleansing for this moment. RATIONALE: Type I provides temporary cleansing that naturally fades. When you need to be clean for a specific purpose but don't want permanent purification, Type I clears without creating ongoing maintenance.

Function

Dissolves foreign energies for this specific clearing. The purification completes its work and naturally releases, returning you to normal permeability. Does not create ongoing maintenance--simply clears what needs clearing now.

Charge

All that is not mine dissolves--now, for this purpose, in this moment. I clear the residue of what I have encountered and return to myself, clean enough for what comes next. This purification completes itself and asks nothing further. I am cleansed. The work is done. Normal life resumes.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the temporary cleansing has served its purpose and even its light residue can release. Use when you want to fully return to normal permeability and accumulation. Generally unnecessary--Type I naturally fades--but available if you want to actively close the cleansing cycle.

H: Red to Black (Class +1) E: Fire to Water (Class +/-2) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Black to Green (Class +/-2) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible release of cleansing residue into normal flow. RATIONALE: Type I reversal actively closes the cycle if desired. Generally unnecessary since the main working naturally fades, but available for clean closure.

Function

Actively releases any remaining cleansing influence, returning fully to normal energetic exchange. The purification cycle closes completely.

Reversal Charge

The cleansing is complete and releases fully. Any lingering purification softens and dissolves; I return to ordinary accumulation, ordinary exchange, ordinary life. The clearing served its moment; now even its echo fades. I am clean enough, and cleanliness gives way to living.

Use Case

When you have been attacked, drained, or damaged by hostile workings, toxic relationships, or overwhelming circumstances. Use after psychic assault, energy vampirism, or any situation that left you depleted, scattered, or wounded. Appropriate when you need active regeneration rather than passive rest.

Function

Transforms damage and depletion into regenerative vitality that blossoms into full sovereign restoration. The healed state locks into place, maintaining wholeness as the new baseline.

Charge

From what was broken, vitality rises like green fire. From what was scattered, sovereignty gathers itself and stands. Every wound becomes a wellspring; every loss transforms into strength reclaimed. I do not merely heal--I am remade more whole than before. My restoration is complete, and completeness maintains itself.

Reversal Configuration

Reversal Charge

8.2 Sovereignty Establishment

Operations that create, maintain, and reinforce your protected domain.

8.2.1a Sanctuary Establishment

Creating sovereign space where peace is maintained and borders respected

Use Case

When establishing a new protected space--your home, office, ritual space, or any location that should be sovereign territory. Use when moving to a new place, after clearing a compromised space, or when you need to claim territory as definitively yours. Appropriate for creating lasting protective boundaries that require no ongoing attention.

Working Configuration

H: Red to White (Class +/-2) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: White to Red (Class +/-2) T: Red to White (Class +/-2) Type III Mirror Inversion Self-correcting sovereignty loop; purity and authority sustain each other. RATIONALE: Mirror Inversion creates a self-correcting feedback loop where purity maintains authority and authority maintains purity. The sanctuary doesn't just persist--it actively corrects violations without your attention.

Function

Creates a sovereign sanctuary where peace maintains itself, borders are automatically enforced, and intrusion is structurally prevented. The space becomes yours in the deepest sense--self-correcting and self-sustaining.

Charge

This space is mine, and mine alone. Peace is not requested here--it is enforced by the very stones, the very air, the very fabric of what this place has become. What enters does so by my will; what remains does so by my permission. The boundaries know themselves and correct any violation without my attention. I am sovereign here, and sovereignty maintains itself.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When you are leaving a space permanently and want to release your claim on it. Use when moving out, selling property, or ending your relationship with a location. Appropriate when the sanctuary has served its purpose and you want to return the space to neutral rather than leave your sovereignty locked in walls you no longer inhabit.

H: Black to Green (Class +/-2) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Green to Black (Class +/-2) T: Green to Black (Class +/-2) Type III (Destination Locking) Dissolution of sanctuary structure into neutral space. RATIONALE: Type III locks the dissolution as the new state of the space. You want neutral ground to remain neutral, not to drift back toward your old sovereignty pattern.

Function

Dissolves the sovereign sanctuary structure, returning the space to neutral ground. The self-maintaining boundaries release, and the space becomes ordinary once more.

Reversal Charge

I release this sanctuary, for its purpose is served. The boundaries dissolve like morning mist; the enforced peace softens to mere possibility. This space returns to what it was before I claimed it--neutral ground, open territory, belonging to no one and everyone. I carry my sovereignty with me; I need not leave it locked in walls. The sanctuary dissolves, and I am free.

8.2.1b Sanctuary Establishment - Type IV Alternative

Absolute Sanctuary

Use Case

When establishing sanctuary that must NEVER be compromised under any circumstances. Use for permanent residence you intend to hold for life, sacred temple space dedicated to ongoing work, or generational family home meant to protect descendants. Appropriate only when you are certain this space will remain yours and you want protections sealed beyond reversal.

WARNING: Type IV is extremely difficult to reverse. Use only when permanence is genuinely desired. For most situations, Type III is sufficient and safer.

Working Configuration

H: Red to White (Class +/-2) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Red to White (Class +/-2) T: Red to White (Class +/-2) Type IV (Absolute Identity) Sealed sovereignty; sanctuary becomes permanent law of this space. RATIONALE: Type IV creates total fixation where change becomes structurally impossible. The sanctuary isn't maintained--it simply IS. Use only when you want protection that cannot be compromised under any circumstances.

Function

Creates absolutely permanent sanctuary. The space becomes sovereign territory in the deepest possible sense--the protection is not maintained, it simply IS. Reversal would require extraordinary effort. The sanctuary is sealed.

Charge

This space is mine eternally. Not maintained, not renewed, not reinforced--simply and absolutely mine, beyond question, beyond challenge, beyond change. The sovereignty I establish here is not a working but a fact, written into the fabric of this place forever. What I have made sacred remains sacred. This sanctuary is sealed.

Reversal Configuration (Multi-Phase Required)

Use Case: When--against all expectation--you must release an absolute sanctuary. This is extraordinarily difficult and should rarely be attempted. Use only if circumstances have fundamentally changed and the sealed space must be returned to neutral. Requires significant sustained effort across multiple phases.

WARNING: Type IV reversal requires multi-phase approach. A single working cannot safely undo absolute sanctuary. Follow all phases in sequence.

Phase 1: Dissolution (1-7 days maximum)

H: Black to White (Class +1) E: Earth to Water (Class -1) I: Red to White (Class +/-2) T: Black to White (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Dissolution with purification exit; begins structural breakdown. RATIONALE: Type II builds from dissolution (the origin) toward purification. This weakens the seal progressively rather than trying to shatter it all at once, which could cause backlash.

Phase 1 Function

Initiates dissolution of the sealed sanctuary while maintaining exit toward purification. The Host provides developmental dissolution (not fixated void). This weakens the seal without creating perpetual breakdown.

Phase 1 Charge

The seal begins to soften. What was made absolute now admits the possibility of change. Dissolution touches the edges of this sovereignty, and purification follows the breaking. The eternal becomes temporal once more. This is the first breath of release.

Phase 2: Neutralization (after Phase 1 completes)

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Black to White (Class +1) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Purification opening to generative neutrality; space returns to potential. RATIONALE: Type II continues the progressive approach, building from purification toward neutral growth. The space returns to open potential rather than being locked into a new pattern.

Phase 2 Function

Completes the dissolution and returns the space to neutral generative potential. What was sealed in sovereignty is now open possibility, neither claimed nor protected.

Phase 2 Charge

The dissolution is complete; now growth returns to this space. Not my growth--simply growth, possibility, the return of potential. This space belongs to no one now. What I sealed, I have unsealed. What I claimed, I release. The sanctuary dissolves into neutral ground, ready for whatever comes next.

Operations governing what crosses your thresholds and how.

Use Case

When a bond must be severed with absolute finality--not merely cut but made impossible to ever reform. Use for the most toxic connections, bonds with those who have caused severe harm, or situations where any possibility of reconnection poses genuine danger. Appropriate only when you are certain you never want this bond to exist again under any circumstances.

EXTREME CAUTION - "THE VOID LOCK": This configuration uses triple Black→Black (Class 0) Type IV--known as "The Void Lock." It creates perpetual dissolution as fixed law. This is appropriate ONLY for absolute severance of EXTERNAL bonds, NEVER for self-work or identity-level operations. The dissolution field is confined to the specific bond being severed. Even so, always perform the Integration working (8.1.4) immediately after to seal the wound and prevent the void from expanding.

WARNING: Type IV severance is essentially irreversible. Use only when absolute permanence is genuinely necessary. For most cord-cutting, 8.5.1a (Type II) is sufficient and safer.

Working Configuration

H: Black to Black (Class 0) E: Fire to Air (Class +1) I: Black to Black (Class 0) T: Black to Black (Class 0) Type IV (Absolute Identity) Sealed dissolution; the bond is not merely broken but made impossible. RATIONALE: Type IV creates absolute impossibility of reconnection. When a bond must NEVER reform under any circumstances, Type IV annihilates the very capacity for that specific connection. REQUIRED FOLLOW-UP: Always perform Integration (8.1.4) immediately after to seal the wound created by absolute severance.

Function

Severs the bond with absolute finality. The connection does not merely dissolve--the very possibility of connection is unmade. This is not cord-cutting but cord-annihilation. What was bound cannot be bound again.

Charge

This connection does not merely end--it becomes impossible. The cord is not cut but unmade from the fabric of possibility itself. What bound us never existed; what connected us cannot exist; what might reconnect us is dissolved before it can form. I am not merely free of you--I am incapable of being bound to you again. This severance is absolute, permanent, and sealed.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When--extraordinarily--you need to restore the capacity for connection that was absolutely severed. This does NOT restore the specific bond that was cut; it restores the possibility of bonding in that area of your being. Use only if the absolute severance has created unintended incapacity for healthy connection. Extremely difficult.

WARNING: Type IV severance reversal is extraordinarily arduous. This begins the process of restoring connective capacity but does not guarantee success. Multiple workings may be required.

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Water to Fire (Class +/-2) I: Black to Green (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Generative development restores capacity; growth toward healthy sovereignty in bonding. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative vitality (the origin) toward restored connection capacity. After absolute severance, new bonding ability must grow developmentally rather than being forced into existence.

Function

Restores the capacity for connection through developmental growth rather than fixation. What was dissolved now grows again--not compulsively, but with sovereign choice. The ability to bond returns through generative development, allowing healthy discrimination in future connections.

Reversal Charge

What was made impossible, I make possible again--not the bond itself, but the capacity to bond. From the void, growth returns. From absolute severance, the possibility of connection emerges. I am not compelled to bond, but I am capable once more. The capacity develops within me, growing toward sovereign choice in connection. I can bond if I choose, with whom I choose. The restoration is developmental, not forced.

8.6 Extending Protection

Operations that extend your sovereignty to cover others.

8.6.1 Extension

Protecting others who are within your sovereign space

Use Case

When you need to extend your protection to cover others--family, guests, clients, or anyone who has entered your space and needs shelter. Use when hosting vulnerable people, when your space is serving as sanctuary for others, or when you have explicitly agreed to cover someone. Appropriate for temporary protection that does not permanently bind you to others.

Working Configuration

H: Red to Green (Class -1) E: Earth to Fire (Class +1) I: Red to White (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible extension under sovereignty; does not permanently bind. RATIONALE: Type I provides temporary coverage without permanent binding. When protecting guests or temporary charges, Type I extends your shelter and naturally releases when they depart.

Function

Extends your sovereign protection to cover others within your space. They share your shelter while present; the protection is flexible and does not create permanent binding.

Charge

Those within my space share my protection. My sovereignty extends like a cloak, like a roof, like a shield held over all who shelter here. While you are in my domain, you are covered by my authority. What would harm you must first pass through what guards me. Here, beneath my care, you are safe.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When those under your protection no longer need it or have left your space. Use when guests depart, when the crisis has passed, or when extended protection is draining your resources. Appropriate when others are ready to stand in their own sovereignty and your covering can be withdrawn.

H: White to Black (Class -1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: Red to Green (Class -1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible withdrawal of extended protection. RATIONALE: Type I allows the extension to withdraw cleanly. When those under your protection leave or no longer need covering, Type I releases without creating new patterns.

Function

Withdraws the extended protection, returning others to their own defenses. Your sovereignty contracts to cover only yourself once more.

Reversal Charge

I withdraw my cloak; you stand again in your own power. My protection served while you were here--now you carry your own. I do not abandon you; I release you to your own sovereignty. My shelter contracts to its natural bounds. You are strong enough to stand without my covering; go with what you have gained.

Part IX: Finance Recipes

Dyadic configurations and charges for financial transformation. Organized from innermost clearing work to outermost sovereignty operations.

9.1 Inner Clearing

Operations focused on dissolving internal blocks to financial flow.

9.1.1a Clearing Financial Fear

Confronting and dissolving scarcity shadow

Use Case

When fear dominates your relationship with money - fear of not having enough, fear of losing what you have, fear of asking for fair payment, or fear of financial decisions. Use when anxiety around money prevents clear thinking and right action. Appropriate when scarcity terror lives in your body and distorts your choices.

Working Configuration

H: Black to White (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to Black (Class 0) T: Black to White (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Purified dissolution becomes self-maintaining; fear cannot reassemble. RATIONALE: Type III locks the purified state so fear cannot reform. Financial fear tends to reassemble from scattered pieces--destination locking prevents this reconstitution. Note: The Initial (I) Black→Black represents the CURRENT frozen fear state being transformed, not a state being created. The Host and Terminal provide the developmental exit toward purification.

Function

Takes the frozen fear state (Black→Black fixation) and transforms it through dissolution into purification. The cleared state locks into place, making fear's return structurally difficult. What was terror becomes calm clarity.

Charge

The fear of not-enough dissolves in my attention. Every scarcity terror, every panic about money, every inherited dread of poverty - I see it, and seeing it, I release it to entropy. What remains is purified clarity where fear once lived. I am not afraid of money or its absence. Financial peace maintains itself in me now.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the fear-clearing has completed its work and you want to restore normal emotional responsiveness to financial matters. Use if the clearing has left you too detached from healthy financial caution, or when the intensity of the dissolution work can soften. Appropriate when peace is established and the fierce clearing can rest.

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Fire to Air (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Vital sovereignty becomes the new self-maintaining baseline. RATIONALE: Type III locks generative sovereignty as your new relationship with money. You don't want to drift back toward either fear or artificial detachment--vital engagement becomes the stable baseline.

Function

Releases the active dissolution field and establishes generative sovereignty as the new baseline. You retain the cleared state but are no longer in active clearing mode.

Reversal Charge

The dissolution has done its work; fear is cleared. I release the fierce purifying and settle into generative sovereignty. My relationship with money is now vital, growing, and fully mine. I no longer need to clear what is already gone. Financial peace is simply who I am.

9.1.1b Clearing Financial Fear - Type I Alternative

Immediate Crisis Calm

Use Case

When you need to calm financial panic for a specific situation rather than permanently dissolving deep-seated fear. Use before a major financial decision, during a crisis that requires clear thinking NOW, or when acute anxiety is blocking immediate action. Appropriate when you need to function through fear for this moment without committing to deep therapeutic work.

Working Configuration

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to White (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible fear-clearing that calms for this situation and releases. RATIONALE: Type I provides temporary calm for a specific crisis. When you need clear thinking NOW without committing to deep therapeutic work, Type I calms the panic and naturally releases.

Function

Dissolves acute financial fear for this specific moment. The panic subsides enough for clear thinking and right action. Does not permanently restructure your relationship with financial fear--simply calms what needs calming now so you can function.

Charge

The fear quiets--now, for this decision, for this moment. I do not need to dissolve all my scarcity terror today; I need to think clearly right now. The panic subsides enough for wisdom to function. I am calm enough for what is before me. This clearing serves the moment and asks nothing permanent. I can act; the fear will wait.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the immediate crisis has passed and even the light calming can release. Generally unnecessary--Type I naturally fades--but available if you want to actively close the calming and return to your baseline relationship with financial anxiety.

RATIONALE: Type I reversal actively closes the calming if it persists. Generally unnecessary since Type I naturally fades, but available for explicit return to baseline.

Function

Actively releases the calming field, returning to your baseline emotional state around money. The crisis clearing completes.

Reversal Charge

The crisis has passed; the calming releases. I return to my ordinary relationship with financial matters--whatever that is, it is mine. The emergency clarity served its purpose; now normal feeling returns. I am no longer in crisis mode. Life resumes its usual texture.

Working Configuration
