RATIONALE: Type III locks the open channel so deflection patterns cannot reassert. Without destination locking, old habits of refusing prosperity tend to return--Type III makes receiving automatic.

Function

Dissolves the blocks to receiving and opens the channel for money to flow in. Generative energy grows into sovereign expression - receiving becomes an act of authority, not passivity. The open channel maintains itself.

Charge

I open to receive. Every block that deflected abundance, every pattern that refused prosperity, every way I stopped money at the threshold - dissolved. The channel is clear; the door is open. Money flows to me now because I allow it. I receive fully, freely, and without apology. What comes to me is welcome, and much is coming.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the opening is complete and the intense receptivity can normalize. Use if being constantly open to receive has become grasping or depleting. Appropriate when the channel is clear and natural flow can replace active opening.

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Earth to Water (Class -1) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to purified generativity without locked receiving. RATIONALE: Type II builds from purified growth (the origin) into natural flow. You retain the clear channel while releasing the active pulling--receiving becomes presence rather than effort.

Function

Releases the intensified opening and establishes natural receptivity. The channel stays clear but you're not in active receiving mode.

Reversal Charge

The channel is clear; I release the intense opening. I remain receptive without straining to receive. Natural flow replaces active pulling. Money comes because the way is open, not because I am always reaching. I trust the cleared channel to function without my constant attention. I receive by being available, not by effort.

9.4.1b Opening to Receive - Type I Alternative

Opening for Specific Opportunity

Use Case

When you want to open your receiving channels for a specific opportunity rather than permanently maintaining heightened receptivity. Use when a particular income source is approaching, during a defined fundraising or sales period, or when preparing for a specific windfall. Appropriate when you need to be extra-receptive NOW but prolonged openness would become grasping or depleting.

Working Configuration

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Fire (Class +/-2) I: Black to Green (Class +/-2) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible opening that receives this opportunity and releases. RATIONALE: Type I provides temporary heightened receptivity for a specific window. When you need to be extra-open NOW without maintaining constant receiving mode, Type I opens and naturally closes.

Function

Opens receiving channels for this specific opportunity window. Blocks dissolve, receptivity heightens, and what is coming can arrive. The opening serves its purpose and naturally closes when the opportunity has been received or passed.

Charge

I open to receive what is coming--now, this opportunity, this window. The channels clear for what approaches. I am receptive without grasping, open without desperate. What is meant to arrive finds welcome. When this passes, I may close again to normal flow. The opening serves the moment and releases.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the opportunity has arrived or passed and the heightened opening can close. Generally unnecessary--Type I naturally releases--but available if the intense receptivity is persisting into anxious grasping.

H: Red to White (Class +/-2) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible closing of opportunity window into normal flow. RATIONALE: Type I reversal actively closes the heightened opening if it persists. Generally unnecessary since Type I naturally releases, but available if receptivity lingers into grasping.

Function

Actively closes the heightened receptivity, returning to normal receiving capacity. The opportunity window served; ordinary flow resumes.

Reversal Charge

The window closes; the heightened opening releases. What came has come; what did not was not meant for this time. I return to normal receptivity--neither grasping nor closed, simply present. The intense opening served its purpose. Normal abundance flow is enough.

9.4.1c Opening to Receive - Type II Alternative

Momentum-Based Opening

Use Case

When you want to build receiving capacity progressively rather than either temporarily (Type I) or permanently (Type III). Use when opening channels through a sustained process--building a client base, developing income streams over months, or systematically increasing earning capacity. Appropriate when the opening is a PROCESS rather than a single moment or permanent installation.

Working Configuration

H: Black to Green (Class +/-2) E: Water to Fire (Class +/-2) I: Black to Green (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Momentum from dissolving blocks carries the opening forward progressively. RATIONALE: Type II creates progressive opening where each cleared block fuels further opening. When receptivity is a process rather than a moment, Type II sustains momentum from an established base.

Function

Creates progressive opening of receiving channels, building momentum from the dissolution of each block. Each cleared obstacle fuels further opening. The process sustains itself while you're actively working it but doesn't lock permanently--it carries force from the ongoing clearing work.

Charge

I dissolve the blocks to receiving, and each dissolution opens me further. The momentum builds--each cleared fear, each released pattern, each removed obstacle adds to the opening. I am in process, progressively more receptive, building capacity through sustained clearing. This is not a single opening but a developing one. The work continues; the channels widen.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the progressive opening has served and you want to stabilize at your current capacity. Use when the channel-clearing process is complete for now and you want to rest in what you've opened without continuing to push further.

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Red to White (Class +/-2) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Sovereign manifestation stabilizes what was opened. RATIONALE: Type II shifts from progressive opening to stable holding. You keep what you've gained without continuing to push--the opened capacity becomes the new base for manifestation.

Function

Shifts from progressive opening to stable holding. What has been opened remains open; the momentum-building ceases. You keep what you've gained without pushing further.

Reversal Charge

The opening has progressed far enough for now. I stabilize at this capacity, holding what I have opened without pushing further. The momentum served; now I rest in expanded receptivity. What I can receive, I can receive. The progressive work pauses; I consolidate my gains. There will be time for further opening later.

Aligning daily experience with freely usable, consequence-free extra money

Use Case

When you want consistent daily financial increase - not windfalls but reliable flow of freely usable money through many avenues. Use to dissolve fear and limiting beliefs while opening to abundant channels. Use when you want abundance to be daily experience, not occasional luck. Appropriate when you are ready to receive at least $20/day as natural, embodied expression rather than effortful pursuit.

Working Configuration

RATIONALE: Type I provides the transformational crucible that completes and releases. Daily abundance becomes natural expression--the working installs the pattern and lets you live it.

Function

Through a Black-to-Green crucible, dissolves limiting financial beliefs and nurtures generative openness. Using Water-to-Fire method, receives opportunities fluidly and energizes them into action. The graft moves from clarified growth (White-to-Green) to manifested abundance (Green-to-Red). Daily financial increase becomes natural expression.

Charge

I dissolve all constriction around money and open fully to generative, embodied abundance. Each day brings freely usable financial increase, arriving through unlimited and unexpected paths. I welcome this flow with ease, clarity, and sovereign manifestation. At least $20 each day flows to me naturally. I do not pursue abundance - I embody it.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the daily flow is established and the active dissolution field can release. Use when abundance has become natural enough that the crucible is no longer needed. Appropriate when you want to maintain the flow without the intensity of active belief-clearing.

H: Red to White (Class +/-2) E: Earth to Air (Class +/-2) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: Red to Green (Class -1) Type I (Linear Transition) Transition from active manifestation to stable abundance maintenance. RATIONALE: Type I allows the intense manifestation to settle into normal living. When abundance is established, you no longer need the transformational crucible--ordinary flow continues naturally.

Function

Releases the dissolution crucible and the intense manifestation field, establishing calm sovereign stability as the new mode. The flow continues but without the transformational intensity.

Reversal Charge

The abundance flows; the crucible has done its work. I release the active dissolution and the intense manifesting. Daily prosperity is now simply my life, requiring no special attention. The channels are established; the beliefs are cleared; the flow continues naturally. I rest in abundance rather than creating it. What was working has become simply living.

9.4.3 Generosity Flow

Healthy giving without depletion

Use Case

When you want to give freely but fear giving will deplete you, or when you hoard from fear and want to circulate freely instead. Use to establish generous flow that replenishes rather than drains. Appropriate when you understand that circulation increases abundance but need to embody this truth.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign generosity becomes self-maintaining circulation. Function

Establishes generosity as a self-replenishing flow. Purified intention grows into sovereign expression - giving that comes from fullness, not depletion. Emotional flow grounds into stable circulation. The generous stance maintains itself, and giving increases rather than decreases your abundance.

Charge

I give from fullness, and giving increases my fullness. Generosity flows through me like water through a spring - the more that flows out, the more flows in. I release the hoarding that came from fear; I circulate freely because circulation is abundance. My giving depletes nothing; it opens channels. I am generous, and generosity makes me more.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the generous flow is established and you need to restore appropriate boundaries. Use if generosity has become compulsive or if others are draining you through your openness. Appropriate when you need to balance giving with wise holding.

RATIONALE: Type II builds from sovereign clarity (the origin) into wise discernment. You remain capable of giving while restoring the ability to hold wisely when that serves better.

Function

Releases the locked generosity flow and restores discerning sovereignty. You remain capable of giving but are not in constant circulation mode.

Reversal Charge

The generosity served; now I restore appropriate boundaries. I release the constant flow and return to sovereign discernment. I can give and I can hold; both are expressions of abundance. The compulsive circulation softens to wise choice. I am generous when generosity serves, and wisely boundaried when that serves better.

9.5 Accumulation and Protection

Operations for building, holding, and protecting financial resources.

9.5.1a Wealth Accumulation

Stable growth and building reserves

Use Case

When you want to build wealth over time - not just flow but accumulation, not just enough but reserves and growth. Use when you're ready to move from sufficiency to prosperity, from having enough to having more than enough. Appropriate for building lasting financial foundation.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Earth to Fire (Class +1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type IV (Absolute Identity) Total generative-sovereign lock; accumulation becomes structural. RATIONALE: Type IV creates absolute alignment toward wealth building. When you want accumulation to be structural reality rather than ongoing effort, total fixation prevents any drift from the building pattern.

Function

Creates absolute alignment toward wealth accumulation - growth manifesting into sovereign holdings at every level. This is a building configuration, designed to lock in accumulation as structural reality.

Charge

Wealth accumulates in my life as natural law. What comes to me grows; what I hold increases; what I build compounds. I am not merely surviving or sufficient - I am prospering, accumulating, building lasting abundance. This growth is locked into my structure now. Wealth builds upon wealth, and I am someone whose resources grow.

Reversal Configuration (Multi-Phase Required)

Use Case: When the accumulation phase is complete or when the locked building energy needs to release. Use when you have enough accumulated and want to shift from building to enjoying or circulating. Appropriate when the intensity of accumulation has served and life asks for different relationship with wealth. Requires significant sustained effort across multiple phases.

WARNING: Type IV reversal requires multi-phase approach. A single working cannot safely undo absolute wealth accumulation lock. Follow all phases in sequence.

Phase 1: Loosening the Lock (1-7 days)

H: Black to White (Class +1) E: Earth to Water (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Black to White (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Dissolution with purification exit; begins separating identity from pattern. RATIONALE: Type II builds from dissolution (the origin) toward clarity. This loosens identification with accumulation while maintaining the actual wealth--you begin to have rather than be your prosperity.

Phase 1 Function

Initiates dissolution of the absolute identification while maintaining the Green→Red graft (the actual accumulation pattern). The Host provides developmental dissolution--you begin to see the accumulation as pattern rather than self. Purification exit prevents nihilistic void.

Phase 1 Charge

The absolute lock begins to soften. I am not my accumulation--I have accumulated. The pattern served me; it is not me. Dissolution touches the edges of this identity, and I begin to see myself as separate from what I have built. I remain wealthy; I release being wealth itself.

Phase 2: Establishing Flow Capacity (after Phase 1 completes)

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Red to White (Class +/-2) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Purification opening to generative flexibility; sovereignty releases to growth. RATIONALE: Type II continues from clarity toward flexible relationship. You retain the wealth while gaining freedom to accumulate or circulate as life asks.

Phase 2 Function

Completes the separation and establishes new relationship with wealth. What was locked as "I am accumulating" becomes "I can accumulate or circulate as I choose." The sovereign lock releases into generative potential.

Phase 2 Charge

The lock releases; I am free to choose. Wealth remains--it is mine, not me. I can build and I can flow; I can hold and I can release. The absolute accumulation softens to sovereign choice. I have built well. Now I may enjoy, give, circulate, or continue building as life asks. The structure remains; the identification dissolves.

9.5.1b Wealth Accumulation - Type III Alternative

Ongoing Accumulation

Use Case

When you want wealth accumulation that maintains itself but remains adjustable--not absolutely locked. Use when building wealth over time with the understanding that life circumstances may change and you may need to shift from accumulation to circulation or enjoyment. Appropriate when you want lasting accumulation tendency without permanent structural freezing.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Earth to Fire (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign accumulation becomes self-maintaining but remains reversible. RATIONALE: Type III makes accumulation your baseline orientation while preserving your sovereignty over the pattern. Unlike Type IV, you retain the authority to adjust when life circumstances change.

Function

Creates self-maintaining wealth accumulation--the pattern of building continues without constant attention. Growth becomes sovereignty becomes the environmental law. Unlike Type IV, this can be consciously reversed when life circumstances call for different relationship with wealth.

Charge

Wealth accumulates in my life as continuing pattern. What comes to me grows; what I hold increases. I am building, accumulating, creating lasting abundance. This growth maintains itself as my baseline orientation. Yet I remain sovereign over this pattern--it serves me, not I it. Accumulation continues; I retain the authority to adjust.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the accumulation phase is complete or when life calls for circulation rather than building. Use when you have enough and want to shift to enjoying, giving, or simply living without the accumulation orientation. Appropriate when the building served and now something else is needed.

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Red to Green (Class -1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Generative clarity as base releases into softened prosperity. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative clarity (the origin) toward flexible relationship with wealth. You retain abundance while gaining freedom to flow, circulate, or enjoy as life asks.

Function

Releases the self-maintaining accumulation pattern. Resources can now flow as well as build. The orientation shifts from "always building" to "flowing as appropriate." The origin reinforcement provides stable grounding while allowing movement away from locked accumulation.

Reversal Charge

The accumulation has served; I have built well. I release the building pattern and allow wealth to flow again. I can hold and I can release; I can build and I can circulate. The accumulation orientation softens to responsive prosperity. I have enough. I may enjoy, give, or simply live without the constant building. The pattern releases; abundance remains.

I refuse drains, leaks, and unwise expenditures - not through constant vigilance but through boundaries that know themselves. My resources are guarded by sovereign clarity. What would deplete me is turned away; what would waste me is refused.

Reversal Configuration

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Red to Green (Class -1) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible generative clarity replaces locked boundaries. 9.5.3 Financial Sovereignty

Authority over your earning and resources

Use Case

When your financial life is controlled by others - bosses, markets, circumstances, systems. Use when you want to claim authority over your own earning and resources rather than being at the mercy of external forces. Appropriate when you're ready to move from financial dependence to financial self-determination.

PREREQUISITE: This working uses Red→Red (Class 0) fixation to lock sovereignty. To avoid "Premature Throne" risk (claiming authority without foundation), complete foundational work first: 9.1 Inner Clearing, 9.2 Mindset Installation, and 9.3 Capacity Building. Sovereignty claimed without these foundations may collapse when tested.

Working Configuration

H: Red to Red (Class 0) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Red to Red (Class 0) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign lock; financial self-determination becomes structural. RATIONALE: Type III locks sovereignty as identity-level truth. After completing foundational work, your financial self-determination should maintain itself as environmental law, not something requiring constant assertion. Note: Red→Red fixation is appropriate here because you are locking sovereignty that has been BUILT through prior developmental work. Do not use this as a shortcut to skip the building process.

Function

Creates absolute financial sovereignty - authority over your earning and resources that cannot be taken. This is an identity-level installation, making self-determination the structural truth of your financial life.

Charge

I am sovereign over my financial life. No one controls my earning but me; no one determines my prosperity but me. I am not at the mercy of bosses, markets, or circumstances - I am the authority in my own financial domain. This sovereignty is locked into my structure. I earn by my will; I hold by my choice; I grow by my determination. I am financially self-determined.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the sovereignty is established and the absolute lock can release into more collaborative relationship. Use if total self-determination has become isolation from beneficial partnership. Appropriate when you want to retain authority while allowing healthy interdependence.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Fire (Class +/-2) I: Red to Green (Class -1) T: White to Green (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible movement from absolute sovereignty to generative partnership. RATIONALE: Type I allows sovereignty to soften into collaborative relationship. When self-determination becomes isolation, Type I releases the absolute lock while preserving core authority.

Function

Releases the absolute sovereignty lock while retaining core self-determination. You remain the authority but can collaborate and receive support.

Reversal Charge

My sovereignty is established; I release the isolation. I am still the authority over my financial life, but I can partner now, collaborate, receive support without losing myself. The absolute lock softens to confident self-determination that welcomes beneficial alliance. I am sovereign and I am not alone. Authority includes the power to choose partnership.

End of Part IX: Finance Recipes

Part X: Self-Development Recipes

Dyadic configurations and charges for personal growth and transformation. Organized from inner honesty work through cultivation of new capacities.

10.1 Self-Honesty

Operations focused on seeing yourself clearly and integrating all parts.

10.1.1a Radical Self-Honesty

Dissolving self-deception and seeing clearly

Use Case

When you suspect you're lying to yourself about something important - your motivations, your situation, your patterns, your desires. Use when comfortable illusions prevent necessary change. Appropriate when you're ready to see what you've been avoiding, even if it's uncomfortable.

Working Configuration

H: Black to White (Class +1) E: Air to Water (Class +1) I: Green to Black (Class +/-2) T: Black to White (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Purified dissolution becomes self-maintaining clarity; self-deception cannot reassemble. RATIONALE: Type III locks clarity as your new state. Self-deception tends to rebuild comfortable illusions--destination locking prevents you from easily returning to not-knowing.

Function

Dissolves the comfortable lies and reveals what's underneath. The illusions that protected you from uncomfortable truth are cleared, and what remains is purified clarity about yourself. This clarity maintains itself - you cannot easily return to not-knowing.

Charge

I choose to see myself truly. Every comfortable lie, every protective illusion, every story I tell myself to avoid the real - dissolved in my attention. I am ready to know what I have hidden from myself. The truth may be uncomfortable, but it is mine, and I claim it. Self-honesty maintains itself in me now; I cannot unknow what I know.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the radical honesty has done its work and the fierce seeing can soften. Use if constant self-scrutiny has become harsh or destabilizing. Appropriate when truth is established and gentleness can return.

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Vital sovereignty becomes the new baseline; honesty with kindness. RATIONALE: Type III locks gentle knowing as the new state. You retain clarity while establishing warmth rather than harshness as the mode of self-awareness.

Function

Releases the fierce dissolution and establishes generative sovereignty. You retain clarity but hold it with warmth rather than harshness.

Reversal Charge

The seeing is complete; I know myself truly now. I release the fierce scrutiny and settle into gentle knowing. Honesty need not be harsh to be real. I hold my truth with kindness, seeing clearly without cruelty. Self-knowledge lives in me as warmth, not judgment.

Examination Period

Meeting and integrating disowned parts

Use Case

When parts of yourself have been exiled - qualities you've rejected, emotions you've suppressed, aspects you've deemed unacceptable. Use when these disowned parts create problems by operating unconsciously. Appropriate when you're ready to reclaim what you've pushed away and become whole.

You are not my enemy; you are my lost self returning. In the dissolution, we meet; in the growth, we integrate. I am whole now, shadow and all.

Accurate self-assessment without inflation or deflation

End of Part X: Self-Development Recipes

Part XI: Love Recipes

Dyadic configurations and charges for romantic and relational transformation. Organized from inner preparation through deepening of connection.

11.1 Inner Preparation

Operations focused on preparing yourself for love.

11.1.1 Cultivating Self-Love

Building the foundation all other love rests upon

Use Case

When you struggle to love yourself - when self-criticism dominates, when you treat yourself worse than you'd treat others, when you don't believe you're worthy of love. Use when the absence of self-love undermines all relationships. Appropriate as foundational work before seeking or deepening external love.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Black to Green (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign self-love becomes self-maintaining foundation. RATIONALE: Type III locks self-love as structural foundation. Self-criticism tends to reassert under stress--destination locking ensures self-care becomes your baseline rather than something you have to maintain.

Function

Dissolves the blocks to self-love and grows genuine care for yourself into sovereign expression. Self-love becomes structural - not something you practice but something you are. This foundation maintains itself.

Charge

I love myself. Not as achievement or affirmation but as simple truth - I am worthy of my own care, my own kindness, my own fierce protection. Every block to self-love dissolves; what grows in its place is genuine warmth toward myself. I treat myself as I would treat someone I love, because I am someone I love. This love maintains itself; it is my foundation.

Truly hearing another

Use Case

When you struggle to truly listen - when you're planning your response while they're talking, when you can't hear past your own assumptions, when others don't feel heard by you. Use when you want to develop the capacity for genuine receptive presence. Appropriate for deepening intimacy through attention.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Air to Water (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign listening becomes self-maintaining presence. RATIONALE: Type III locks listening capacity so distracted patterns can't return. The mind habitually plans responses instead of receiving--destination locking makes deep presence your default.

Function

Develops and locks in the capacity for deep listening. You become someone who truly hears - not just words but meaning, not just content but heart. This presence maintains itself.

Charge

I listen deeply. Not waiting to speak, not planning my response, not filtering through my assumptions - truly hearing. I give the gift of my full attention. When you speak, I receive. When you share, I am present. My listening is sovereign and complete. You are heard, and being heard by me heals.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When deep listening is established and the intense receptivity can normalize. Use if constant listening has become depleting or if you need to balance receiving with expressing. Appropriate when listening is natural and speaking can rejoin it.

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Earth to Air (Class +/-2) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to purified growth with balanced exchange. RATIONALE: Type II builds from purified awareness (the origin) into balanced communication. When deep listening is established, Type II allows speaking to rejoin receiving in natural flow.

Function

Releases the intense listening into balanced communication. You remain deeply present but also speak and express.

Reversal Charge

I listen well; now I can also speak. The deep hearing is established; now expression can balance it. I receive and I give voice. The conversation flows both ways. I am present when you speak and present when I do. Listening and speaking, receiving and giving.

11.4.3a Cultivating Mutual Respect — Type III

Lasting Honoring — Honoring each other's sovereignty

Use Case

When respect is lacking or eroding in relationship - when contempt creeps in, when you or your partner are diminished rather than honored, when the sacredness of each person is forgotten. Use when you want to establish or restore fundamental respect. Appropriate for relationships where honoring has been lost and you want lasting self-maintaining respect.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Earth to Fire (Class +1) I: White to Red (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Generative sovereignty becomes self-maintaining; respect grows and locks. RATIONALE: Type III locks mutual honoring so contempt can't erode it. Relationships tend to drift toward taking each other for granted--destination locking ensures respect remains the living environment.

Function

Establishes mutual respect through developmental sovereignty rather than fixation. Both partners are honored and the honoring grows--it can adapt as the relationship evolves while maintaining its essential quality. Respect becomes the living environment of the relationship.

Charge

We are both sovereign, and our sovereignty grows together. I honor your wholeness; you honor mine. Neither diminished, neither superior - two complete beings choosing connection. Respect is the living ground we stand on, growing stronger as we grow. I treat you as sacred; I expect to be treated as sacred. This mutual honoring lives and breathes between us.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When respect is established and the absolute structure can allow more flexibility. Use if rigid mutual respect has prevented healthy challenge or playfulness. Appropriate when respect is secure and lighter relating can return.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to generative clarity with flexible honoring. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative clarity (the origin) into playful relating. When respect is secure, Type II allows challenge and irreverence alongside the fundamental honoring.

Function

Softens the absolute respect structure while maintaining its foundation. You can play, challenge, and be irreverent while still fundamentally honoring.

Reversal Charge

Respect is established; now we can play. The foundation is solid; we can dance on it. I honor you absolutely and I can tease you gently. You are sacred and you are also ridiculous. The fierce honoring softens to loving irreverence. We respect each other, and we also laugh.

11.4.3b Cultivating Mutual Respect — Type I Alternative

Developing Honoring

Use Case

When you want to cultivate mutual respect for a specific period of growth rather than establishing permanent structure. Use in newer relationships where respect is developing, during reconciliation periods, or when consciously practicing honoring without committing to permanence. Appropriate when you want to grow respect naturally and see where it leads.

Working Configuration

H: White to Red (Class +/-2) E: Earth to Fire (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible respect development that grows naturally and releases when complete. RATIONALE: Type I provides organic respect cultivation during formative relationship period. When you want to discover what mutual honoring means for you without forcing permanent structure, Type I supports natural development.

Function

Creates a developmental period of mutual respect cultivation. Purification births sovereignty through grounded action, while growth leads to full expression. The respect develops organically and can either be locked in (by following with Type III) or allowed to find its natural level.

Charge

We practice honoring each other during this time of growth. I treat you with respect; you treat me with respect. We are learning what this means between us. This is not permanent structure but living practice. We grow toward sovereignty together, discovering what mutual honoring looks like for us. The respect develops; we let it show us its shape.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the respect development period has completed or when the relationship is taking a different form. Generally unnecessary--Type I naturally fades--but available if you want clean closure on this practice phase.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Red to Green (Class -1) T: Green to White (Class -1) Type I (Linear Transition) Flexible return from respect practice to natural relating. RATIONALE: Type I reversal closes the developmental window gracefully. Generally unnecessary since Type I naturally completes, but available for clean transition to whatever the relationship becomes.

Function

Releases the active respect cultivation, returning to ordinary relating. What was practiced may continue naturally; what doesn't serve will fade.

Reversal Charge

The practice period closes; we return to natural relating. What we learned about honoring stays with us. What we practiced may continue without the structure. We relate now from wherever we have grown to. The cultivation completes; we keep what served and release the rest.

11.5 Deepening

Operations for deepening intimacy and connection.

11.5.1 Deepening Intimacy

Going further into connection

Use Case

When you want to deepen existing intimacy - when surface connection is good but you hunger for more, when you're ready to be more fully known and to more fully know another. Use when the relationship is ready for another level. Appropriate for established connections seeking greater depth.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Water to Fire (Class +/-2) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign depth becomes self-maintaining intimacy. RATIONALE: Type III locks deeper connection as your new baseline. Intimacy tends to drift toward the comfortable surface--destination locking ensures depth remains accessible as your natural relating.

Function

Opens new depths of intimacy and establishes them as the new baseline. What was deep becomes normal; what was hidden becomes shared. This deeper connection maintains itself.

Charge

We go deeper. What was hidden I reveal; what was protected I share. I am ready to be more fully known and to more fully know you. The depths call and we answer. Intimacy that once seemed risky becomes natural. We dwell now in places we only visited before. Depth is home now.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When deepening is complete and the intense intimacy can stabilize. Use if constant depth-seeking has become exhausting or if surface connection needs restoration. Appropriate when you want to enjoy achieved depth rather than always seeking more.

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Earth to Water (Class -1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to purified growth, stabilizing achieved depth. RATIONALE: Type II builds from purified awareness (the origin) into stable intimacy. When depth is achieved, Type II allows resting in connection rather than constantly seeking more.

Function

Releases the intense deepening and stabilizes what's been achieved. You rest in intimacy rather than constantly pursuing more.

Reversal Charge

The depth is achieved; we can rest here. I release the constant seeking of more and enjoy what is. We are intimate; we don't need to prove it by going always deeper. The connection stabilizes at this new level. We dwell in depth without drowning.

11.5.2a Sustaining Passion — Type IV

Lasting Fire — Keeping the fire alive

Use Case

When passion fades or threatens to fade - when familiarity breeds not contempt but boredom, when the fire that began love needs tending. Use when you want to sustain or reignite desire and aliveness in long-term connection. Appropriate for established relationships committed to lasting vitality.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type IV (Absolute Identity) Generative sovereignty locked; passion maintains itself through living growth. RATIONALE: Type IV creates permanent structure that can breathe. Passion needs both stability and evolution--absolute identity in generative sovereignty allows fire to maintain itself through ongoing growth rather than frozen flame.

Function

Locks generative passion into the structure of the relationship. Desire remains alive through ongoing growth--not frozen fire but living flame that renews itself. The passion can breathe and evolve while remaining fundamentally present.

Charge

The fire lives and grows. Not frozen flame but living passion - desire that renews itself through ongoing growth. We are still lit by each other, still sparked by each other, still burning for each other. Time does not cool this fire; it feeds it. Our passion grows as we grow, evolving yet ever-present.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When passion is secured and the intensity can modulate. Use if constant fire has become exhausting or if quieter love needs room. Appropriate when you want passion available but not always dominant.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to generative clarity with balanced fire. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative clarity (the origin) into modulated passion. When fire is secured, Type II allows intensity to wax and wane while maintaining fundamental aliveness.

Function

Releases the locked passion into more modulated aliveness. Fire remains available but doesn't always burn at full intensity.

Reversal Charge

The fire is secured; now it can rest. Passion remains but doesn't consume. We can burn bright and we can simmer. The constant intensity softens to available aliveness. Hot when we choose, warm always. Fire and rest, passion and peace.

11.5.2b Sustaining Passion — Type III Alternative

Renewable Fire

Use Case

When you want lasting passion that maintains itself but can evolve with the relationship--not permanently frozen fire. Use when you want sustained desire without absolute lock, when you recognize that passion may need to transform as life circumstances change, or when you want the fire alive but not forced. Appropriate when you want lasting aliveness without permanence that prevents natural evolution.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: White to Red (Class +/-2) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign passion becomes self-maintaining but remains responsive. RATIONALE: Type III locks passion while allowing evolution. Unlike Type IV's absolute permanence, Type III maintains fire through self-sustaining momentum while remaining responsive to relationship transformation.

Function

Creates self-maintaining passion--desire continues to arise without constant effort. The fire stays lit through its own momentum. Unlike Type IV, this passion can evolve, transform, or be consciously released if the relationship itself transforms.

Charge

The fire lives as ongoing aliveness between us. Passion maintains itself as our way together. We remain lit by each other, still desiring, still alive. This fire sustains itself--and it can also transform if we transform. I commit to passion while allowing it to evolve with us.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When passion has been established and the relationship is transforming to different form. Use when partnership ends, transforms to friendship, or when passion served but quieter love is now appropriate. Appropriate when fire was good and is now complete.

H: White to Green (Class +1) E: Water to Earth (Class +1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to purified growth with peaceful warmth. RATIONALE: Type II builds from purified awareness (the origin) into transformed connection. When passion has served, Type II allows fire to become warmth, desire to become appreciation.

Function

Releases the sustained passion, allowing the relationship to transform to whatever form serves both parties now. Fire becomes warmth, passion becomes affection, desire becomes appreciation.

Reversal Charge

The fire has burned well; now it can transform. Passion releases into warmth. We were lovers; now we are whatever we become. The intensity served; now gentler relating is possible. I release the fire with gratitude for what it gave us. Warmth remains.

11.5.3a Growing Together — Type IV

Absolute Commitment — Evolving in partnership

Use Case

When you want the relationship itself to grow - not just maintaining connection but actively evolving together, becoming more than either could become alone. Use when you're committed to mutual development and CERTAIN of permanent partnership. Appropriate for partnerships dedicated to shared becoming with no possibility of separation.

Working Configuration

H: Green to Red (Class +1) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: Green to Red (Class +1) Type IV (Absolute Identity) Shared growth becomes permanent structure; evolution is locked in. RATIONALE: Type IV makes mutual evolution non-negotiable. Growth together becomes structural--this is for partnerships where constant becoming is the fundamental commitment and separation is not considered possible.

Function

Locks mutual growth into the permanent structure of the relationship. The partnership is committed to evolution - individually and together. This dedication maintains itself absolutely.

Charge

We grow together. Not just staying but becoming - more than we were, more than we could be alone. This relationship is a vehicle for evolution. We make each other more. Growth is not optional in this love; it is structural. We are committed to becoming, and we become together.

Reversal Configuration (Multi-Phase Required)

Use Case: When the locked growth imperative needs to release--either because constant evolution has prevented rest, or because the relationship is ending and paths must diverge. This is extraordinarily difficult and should rarely be attempted. Requires significant sustained effort across multiple phases.

WARNING: Type IV reversal requires multi-phase approach. A single working cannot safely undo absolute growth commitment. Follow all phases in sequence. Choose Phase 2 or Phase 2 Alternative based on whether the relationship continues.

Phase 1: Releasing Growth Compulsion (1-7 days)

H: White to Black (Class -1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Green to Red (Class +1) T: White to Black (Class -1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Purification dissolving into rest; growth imperative softens to presence. RATIONALE: Type II builds from purification (the origin) toward dissolution. The fierce "must evolve" relaxes toward "may rest"--this doesn't destroy growth but releases the compulsion.

Phase 1 Function

Initiates dissolution of the locked growth imperative while maintaining the Green→Red graft (the actual growth orientation). The Host provides regressive purification into dissolution--the fierce "must evolve" softens toward "may rest." This is not destroying the relationship but releasing the compulsion.

Phase 1 Charge

The absolute imperative begins to soften. We do not need to constantly become--we may also simply be. The locked evolution relaxes its grip. We have grown; we may rest in what we've become. Dissolution touches the edges of compulsive transformation. We remain partners; we release the tyranny of endless growth.

Phase 2: Establishing Chosen Evolution (after Phase 1 completes)

Use when relationship continues but growth compulsion needs release.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Earth to Water (Class -1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: Green to White (Class -1) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Growth returns to purified potential; evolution becomes choice rather than structure. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative awareness (the origin) toward chosen partnership. What was locked as "must grow" becomes "may grow if we choose."

Phase 2 Function

Completes the release and establishes new relationship with shared growth. What was locked as "we must grow together" becomes "we may grow together if we choose." The absolute commitment softens to sovereign partnership.

Phase 2 Charge

The lock releases; we are free to choose our pace. Growth remains available--it is our option, not our prison. We can evolve and we can rest; we can become and we can appreciate what we are. The absolute growth imperative softens to loving choice. We have grown well together. Now we may continue, pause, or find new rhythms as our partnership asks. The bond remains; the compulsion dissolves.

Phase 2 Alternative: Separating Paths (after Phase 1 completes)

Use when relationship is ending and paths must diverge cleanly.

H: Black to Green (Class +/-2) E: Fire to Water (Class +/-2) I: Red to Black (Class +1) T: Black to Green (Class +/-2) Type III (Destination Locking) Dissolution into separate generative potential; paths diverge cleanly. RATIONALE: Type III locks the separation so the old pattern doesn't reassert. When growth together must become growth apart, Type III ensures the divergence holds.

Phase 2 Alternative Function

Completes separation of the locked partnership growth. What was "we grow together always" dissolves into "we each grow separately." The Type III locks the separation so the old pattern doesn't reassert.

Phase 2 Alternative Charge

What was joined now separates cleanly. We grew together; now we grow apart. The locked partnership releases into individual paths. I take what I became with you and carry it forward alone. You do the same. We were committed to shared becoming; now we are committed to our own becoming. The bond dissolves; growth continues separately. We part with what we gained, grateful and complete.

11.5.3b Growing Together — Type III Alternative

Ongoing Evolution

Use Case

When you want lasting shared growth that maintains itself but remains adjustable--not absolutely locked. Use when committing to growth in a developing relationship, when you want evolution without permanence, or when life may require individual paths to diverge. Appropriate when you want shared becoming without irreversible structural lock.

Working Configuration

H: White to Red (Class +/-2) E: Fire to Earth (Class -1) I: White to Green (Class +1) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type III (Destination Locking) Sovereign growth commitment becomes self-maintaining but remains adjustable. RATIONALE: Type III locks growth commitment while preserving reversibility. Unlike Type IV's absolute permanence, Type III sustains shared evolution while allowing paths to diverge if needed.

Function

Creates self-maintaining growth orientation--the partnership continues to evolve without constant recommitment. Both partners are dedicated to becoming more. Unlike Type IV, this can be consciously reversed if paths need to diverge.

Charge

We grow together as ongoing commitment. This relationship continues to evolve, to become more, to make us more than we could be alone. Shared growth maintains itself as our way. I commit to our evolution while retaining the wisdom to adjust if our paths diverge. We become together--for now and as long as our paths align.

Reversal Configuration

Use Case: When the shared growth path has completed or needs to diverge. Use when partnership ends or when individual growth requires separate paths. Appropriate when growing together served and growing apart is now right.

H: Green to White (Class -1) E: Water to Air (Class -1) I: Green to White (Class -1) T: White to Red (Class +/-2) Type II (Origin Reinforcement) Return to generative clarity as individuals. RATIONALE: Type II builds from generative clarity (the origin) into individual sovereignty. When shared paths diverge, Type II allows both parties to continue their own evolution with gratitude for shared becoming.

Function

Releases the shared growth commitment, allowing both parties to pursue individual evolution. Gratitude for shared becoming; freedom for separate paths.

Reversal Charge

Our shared path has reached its completion for now. I release the growth commitment with gratitude for what we became together. We grew well; now we may grow separately. The shared evolution served; individual paths call. I wish you growth on your own way. We made each other more; we release each other to continue becoming.

End of Part XI: Love Recipes

Part XII: Working Sequences

Common situations may call for multiple workings in sequence. This section organizes sequences by life domain and common scenarios, drawing from all recipe sections as appropriate.

Note on Type Alternatives

Many workings offer both Type III (lasting) and Type I (temporary) configurations. When using sequences, consider which type best fits the context:

For Specific Events (rituals, trips, single incidents): Use Type I alternatives. These naturally release when the situation passes.

For Ongoing Conditions (lifestyle changes, permanent protection): Use Type III. These self-maintain and require active reversal if you want to undo them.

For Absolute Permanence (sealing spaces forever, irreversible severance): Use Type IV. These are extremely difficult to reverse and should be used rarely.

The sequences below reference workings by their base number (e.g., 8.1.1). Choose the appropriate variant (a or b) based on your specific situation.

• • •

12.1 Protection Sequences

Sequences focused on establishing, maintaining, and restoring safety.

Protection Type Alternatives Reference

8.1.1 Self-Cleansing: Type III (lasting) or Type I (temporary)
8.1.2 Recovery: Type III (deep) or Type I (immediate)
8.2.1 Sanctuary Establishment: Type III (self-maintaining) or Type IV (absolute)
8.2.3 Sanctuary Purging: Type III (lasting) or Type I (one-time)
8.2.4 Portability: Type III (ongoing) or Type I (single journey)
8.3.1 Gatekeeping: Type III (lasting) or Type I (situational)
8.3.2 Reception: Type III (lasting) or Type I (temporary opening)
8.3.3 Filter and Redirect: Type III (lasting) or Type I (situational)
8.4.1 Disrupting Attacks: Type III (ongoing) or Type I (immediate)
8.4.5 Concealment: Type III (lasting) or Type I (temporary)
8.5.1 Bond Breaking: Type III (lasting) or Type IV (absolute)

12.1.1 Establishing New Sanctuary

Permanent home protection installation

Gatekeeping (8.3.1a, Type III) — Install lasting intelligent threshold 4. Reception (8.3.2a, Type III) — Permanent opening to beneficial forces Note: All Type III for lasting home protection that maintains itself. Use 8.2.1b (Type IV) instead if you want absolute permanent sanctuary that cannot be reversed even by you.

12.1.2 After an Attack

Immediate response followed by lasting reinforcement

1. Disrupting Incoming Attacks (8.4.1b, Type I) — Stop THIS assault immediately 2. Recovery (8.1.2b, Type I) — Immediate healing from damage 3. Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Call back scattered energy 4. Sanctuary Maintenance (8.2.2) — Reinforce boundaries Note: Steps 1-2 use Type I for immediate crisis response. If attacks continue or deeper healing is needed, follow up with 8.4.1a and 8.1.2a (Type III) for lasting defense and deep restoration.

12.1.3 After Sanctuary Contamination

One-time purging followed by lasting protection

Gatekeeping (8.3.1a, Type III) — Reinstall lasting thresholds Note: Purging and cleansing use Type I for this specific contamination. Gatekeeping uses Type III to prevent future intrusions. If contamination was severe, consider 8.2.3a (Type III) for lasting purification field.

12.1.4 Ending a Toxic Relationship

Permanent severance with lasting protection

Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Call back what was given 5. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Restore self-relationship Note: Type III Bond Breaking for lasting severance that maintains itself. Use 8.5.1b (Type IV) only for absolute, irreversible severance where you want NO possibility of reconnection, even by your own choice.

12.1.5 Traveling or Working Outside Home

Temporary mobile protection for a specific trip or period

Gatekeeping (8.3.1b, Type I) — Situational discrimination while mobile Note: All Type I for a specific trip that releases when you return home. For ongoing travel (frequent business trips, nomadic lifestyle), use 8.2.4a (Type III) for lasting mobile sovereignty.

12.1.6 Frequent Traveler Protection

Lasting protection for those regularly away from home base

Gatekeeping (8.3.1a, Type III) — Permanent discrimination capacity 4. Reception (8.3.2a, Type III) — Always open to beneficial forces Note: All Type III for someone who travels frequently. Mobile protection becomes your normal state rather than temporary heightening.

12.1.7 Welcoming Guests into Protected Space

Temporary opening for specific visitors

Filter and Redirect (8.3.3b, Type I) — Handle any inadvertent intrusions Note: Reception and Filter use Type I because you're opening temporarily for these specific guests. Protection returns to normal after they leave.

12.1.8 Hosting Ongoing Group or Practice

Lasting accommodation for regular gatherings

Filter and Redirect (8.3.3a, Type III) — Permanent transformation capacity 4. Gatekeeping (8.3.1a, Type III) — Lasting intelligent threshold Note: All Type III for regular hosting. Sanctuary Maintenance (8.2.2) — Strengthen home base 5. Recovery (8.1.2a, Type III) — Deep restoration between engagements Note: All Type III for sustained conflict. You need lasting defenses, not temporary heightening. Type III Recovery ensures continuous healing.

12.1.10 Single Hostile Encounter

Immediate response to a specific threat that then passes

Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear residue from encounter Note: All Type I for a single incident. Defenses heighten for this encounter and release when threat passes, avoiding permanent war footing.

Deep, lasting transformation of entire energetic configuration

Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Deep, lasting purification 5. Sanctuary Purging (8.2.3a, Type III) — Lasting purification of space 6. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Rebuild from clean foundation Note: All Type III for complete reset. This is lasting transformation, not temporary clearing. For absolute severance of specific toxic bonds, consider 8.5.1b (Type IV) for step 1.

Fastest possible protection for immediate danger

These activate fast for immediate need and release when crisis passes. Follow up with lasting protections once immediate danger has passed.

12.2.5 Recovering from Financial Crisis

Immediate stabilization followed by lasting protection

1. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1b, Type I) — Address panic NOW 2. Recovery (8.1.2b, Type I) — Immediate healing from shock 3. Breaking Scarcity Patterns (9.1.3) — Prevent crisis from becoming identity 4. Recognizing Financial Opportunity (9.3.2) — Rebuild container 5. Financial Boundaries (9.5.2) — Prevent recurrence Note: Steps 1-2 use Type I for immediate crisis response. Once stabilized, steps 3-5 install lasting protections. If deep fear-clearing is needed after crisis passes, follow up with 9.1.1a (Type III).

12.2.6 Starting a Business or Major Venture

Long-term venture requiring sustained building and permanent sovereignty

1. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1a, Type III) — Remove fear blocks permanently 2. Financial Self-Worth (9.2.2) — Know you deserve success 3. Discernment in Financial Matters (9.3.3a, Type III) — Lasting business judgment 4. Opening to Receive (9.4.1c, Type II) — Build receiving momentum progressively 5. Financial Sovereignty (9.5.3, Type III) — Claim lasting authority over creation Note: Type II Opening builds receiving capacity as the business grows. Type III Discernment provides lasting judgment for ongoing decisions.

12.2.7 Preparing for Salary Negotiation

Targeted preparation for a single high-stakes financial conversation

1. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1b, Type I) — Calm nerves for this meeting 2. Financial Self-Worth (9.2.2) — Know your value 3. Discernment in Financial Matters (9.3.3b, Type I) — Sharp for this negotiation 4. Opening to Receive (9.4.1b, Type I) — Receptive to this specific offer Note: All temporary configurations for a single event. The heightened states serve the negotiation and release afterward.

12.2.8 Building Investment Portfolio

Sustained wealth-building with adjustable accumulation

1. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1a, Type III) — Remove fear of markets 2. Discernment in Financial Matters (9.3.3a, Type III) — Lasting investment judgment 3. Financial Discipline (9.3.1) — Consistent contribution 4. Wealth Accumulation (9.5.1b, Type III) — Ongoing but adjustable accumulation 5. Financial Boundaries (9.5.2) — Protect what you build Note: Type III Wealth Accumulation (not Type IV) allows you to shift from accumulation to enjoyment or circulation when life circumstances change.

Recognizing Opportunity (10.3.2a, Type III) — See new possibilities 4. Commitment to Growth (10.4.2) — Lock in new behaviors Note: All lasting configurations for permanent breakthrough.

12.3.6 Evaluating a Specific Opportunity

Discernment (10.3.1) — Lasting discernment supports the choice Note: Type I for steps 1-2 heightens perception for this specific decision and releases afterward, allowing full commitment to the choice.

Building consistent spiritual/development practice

Integrating profound spiritual experience

Commitment to Growth (10.4.2) — Continue development Note: Step 2 uses Type I for the processing period; intense shadow visibility releases once integration is complete.

12.3.9 Complete Identity Transformation

Fundamental self-reconstruction — lasting change

1. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1a, Type III) — Face the full truth permanently 2. Shadow Integration (10.1.2a, Type III) — Lasting shadow awareness 3. Ego Right-Sizing (10.1.3) — Accept the whole picture 4. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Break limiting structures 5. Integration After Breakthrough (10.4.3) — Become the new self 6. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear residue of old identity Note: Type III for identity-level changes (steps 1-5). Type I for step 6 — clearing old identity residue is transitional, not permanent cleansing mode.

12.3.10 Recovering from Spiritual Crisis

Careful rebuilding after destabilization

1. Recovery (8.1.2b, Type I) — Immediate healing 2. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear confusion 3. Ego Right-Sizing (10.1.3) — Re-establish ground 4. Openness to Magick (10.2.1b, Type I) — Careful, temporary reopening 5. Discernment (10.3.1) — Rebuild lasting discernment Note: Type I for steps 1-2 and especially step 4. After spiritual crisis, you want TEMPORARY, monitored opening — not permanent heightened receptivity. Type I allows careful reopening that can close if destabilization returns.

12.4 Love Sequences

Sequences focused on romantic relationships and deep connection.

Love Type Alternatives Reference

11.2.1 Releasing Attachment Patterns: Type III (lasting) or Type I (dating period)

11.3.2 Attracting Right Relationship: Type III (lasting) or Type I (active seeking)
11.3.3 Boundaries in Love: Type III (lasting) or Type I (careful reopening)
11.4.3 Cultivating Mutual Respect: Type IV (absolute) or Type III (sustainable)
11.5.2 Sustaining Passion: Type IV (eternal) or Type III (renewable)
11.5.3 Growing Together: Type IV (absolute) or Type III (ongoing)

12.4.1 Preparing for New Love

Two approaches depending on timeframe

FOR LASTING TRANSFORMATION: 1. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Establish foundation 2. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Clear the past 3. Releasing Attachment Patterns (11.2.1a, Type III) — Lasting secure patterns 4. Receptivity to Love (11.3.1a, Type III) — Lasting openness 5. Attracting Right Relationship (11.3.2a, Type III) — Lasting magnetism FOR ACTIVE DATING PERIOD: 1. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Establish foundation 2. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Clear the past 3. Releasing Attachment Patterns (11.2.1b, Type I) — Heightened awareness for seeking 4. Receptivity to Love (11.3.1b, Type I) — Open for this window 5. Attracting Right Relationship (11.3.2b, Type I) — Active seeking field Note: Type I alternatives in steps 3-5 create temporary heightened states that release naturally when partnership is found.

12.4.2 Healing After a Breakup

Complete recovery sequence

1. Bond Breaking (8.5.1) — Sever energetic connection 2. Integration (8.1.4) — Seal the wound 3. Releasing Past Relationships (11.2.3) — Complete the connection 4. Forgiveness (11.2.2) — Free yourself from resentment 5. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Heal what was hurt 6. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1) — Clear residual energy 7. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Return to self

12.4.3 Careful Reopening After Betrayal

Using Type I alternatives for protected re-entry into relationship capacity

1. Recovery (8.1.2) — Heal the shock 2. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1) — Clear contamination 3. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Process the wound 4. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Restore foundation Note: Type I for steps 4-5 allows protective sharpness during vulnerable period that softens naturally as trust rebuilds.

12.4.4 Deepening an Existing Relationship

Going further into connection

Growing Together (11.5.3b, Type III) — Evolve in partnership Note: Step 5 uses Type III alternative — adjustable commitment rather than absolute lock allows the relationship to evolve naturally.

12.4.5 Restoring a Troubled Relationship

Rebuilding what was damaged

Honest Communication (11.4.1) — Clear the air 5. Softening the Heart (11.1.2) — Reopen 6. Deepening Intimacy (11.5.1) — Reconnect Note: Step 3 uses Type III alternative — when restoring troubled relationships, adjustable respect is wiser than absolute lock until you're certain the relationship has healed.

12.4.6a Maintaining Long-Term Passion - Committed Couples

For couples certain of permanent commitment

1. Boundaries in Love (11.3.3a, Type III) — Maintain separate selves 2. Sustaining Passion (11.5.2a, Type IV) — Lasting fire 3. Growing Together (11.5.3a, Type IV) — Absolute commitment Note: Type IV creates irreversible bond. Use only when certain.

12.4.6b Maintaining Long-Term Passion - Evolving Couples

For couples wanting lasting passion with room to evolve

1. Boundaries in Love (11.3.3a, Type III) — Maintain separate selves 2. Sustaining Passion (11.5.2b, Type III) — Renewable fire 3. Growing Together (11.5.3b, Type III) — Ongoing evolution Note: Type III allows passion and growth to evolve with life circumstances while still maintaining itself.

12.5 Cross-Domain Sequences

Sequences that integrate workings across multiple life areas. These sequences combine recipes from Protection, Finance, Self-Development, and Love domains to address complex life situations.

Note on Type Selection in Cross-Domain Work

Cross-domain sequences often mix configuration types strategically: Type III for lasting installations (identity shifts, sovereignty, boundaries), Type I for temporary states (processing periods, specific windows), Type IV only for absolute commitments (use sparingly), and Type II for building on existing strengths. When multiple domains intersect, consider whether each component should persist independently or release when the sequence completes.

12.5.1a Complete Life Reset

When starting over after major life upheaval — lasting reconstruction

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Deep, lasting purification 2. Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Gather your scattered power 3. Bond Breaking (8.5.1a, Type III) — Lasting severance of old ties 4. Integration (8.1.4) — Seal all wounds 5. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1a, Type III) — Address money anxiety lastingly 6. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1a, Type III) — See yourself clearly, permanently 7. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Rebuild foundation 8. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Create self-maintaining safe space 9. Openness to Magick (10.2.1a, Type III) — Lasting openness to new possibilities 10. Reception (8.3.2a, Type III) — Welcome what comes next, lasting receptivity

Note: Nearly all Type III. A complete life reset establishes new lasting patterns, not temporary states. The exception would be if you anticipate another major transition soon—in that case, use Type I alternatives for steps 5, 9, and 10 to maintain flexibility.

12.5.1b Complete Life Reset - Transitional Variant

When rebuilding but expecting continued change

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear for this transition 2. Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Gather power 3. Bond Breaking (8.5.1a, Type III) — Lasting severance (old ties stay severed) 4. Integration (8.1.4) — Seal wounds 5. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1b, Type I) — Crisis calm for now 6. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1b, Type I) — Clear seeing for this period 7. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Foundation 8. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Lasting safe space 9. Openness to Magick (10.2.1b, Type I) — Open for this transition period 10. Reception (8.3.2b, Type I) — Temporary heightened receptivity

Note: Mix of Type I (transitional states) and Type III (lasting structures). Bond breaking and sanctuary remain lasting; clearing and opening are temporary for this transition period.

12.5.2a Preparing for Major Life Transition

Career change, relocation, or life phase shift — temporary heightened states

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear for this transition 2. Ego Right-Sizing (10.1.3) — Honest self-assessment 3. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Break what holds you back 4. Openness to Divine Knowledge (10.2.2b, Type I) — Open for this transition 5. Portability (8.2.4b, Type I) — Protection for this journey 6. Opening to Receive (9.4.1b, Type I) — If financial transition involved 7. Receptivity to Love (11.3.1b, Type I) — If relationship transition involved 8. Cultivating Discipline (10.4.1) — Build needed capacities

Note: Steps 1, 4-7 use Type I—these create temporary heightened states for the transition that naturally release when you've settled. Step 8 uses Type III because discipline should persist beyond the transition.

12.5.2b Preparing for Major Life Transition - Permanent Shift

When the transition IS the new life (retirement, emigration, complete career change)

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Deep, lasting purification 2. Ego Right-Sizing (10.1.3) — Honest self-assessment 3. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Break old constraints 4. Openness to Divine Knowledge (10.2.2a, Type III) — Lasting receptivity 5. Portability (8.2.4a, Type III) — Ongoing mobile sovereignty 6. Opening to Receive (9.4.1a, Type III) — If financial transition involved 7. Receptivity to Love (11.3.1a, Type III) — If relationship transition involved 8. Cultivating Discipline (10.4.1) — Build needed capacities

Note: All Type III. This IS the new permanent state.

12.5.3 Recovering from Trauma

After severe life disruption — immediate recovery then lasting patterns

1. Recovery (8.1.2b, Type I) — Immediate healing now 2. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear contamination for now 3. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Create lasting safety 4. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Process the wound 5. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1b, Type I) — Face what happened (temporary intensity) 6. Shadow Integration (10.1.2b, Type I) — Process period for impact 7. Integration After Breakthrough (10.4.3) — Integrate the experience 8. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Restore self-relationship

Note: Steps 1-2 and 5-6 use Type I for the immediate processing period. Intense self-examination and shadow visibility should release once integration is complete. Step 3 uses Type III—lasting safety is essential after trauma. If trauma response persists, consider upgrading steps 1-2 to Type III alternatives.

12.5.4a Launching a Creative Project

Starting a book, business, art, or venture — project-specific states

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Clear for this project 2. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1a, Type III) — Lasting clearing if money involved 3. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1b, Type I) — Face creative blocks for this project 4. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Clear limiting beliefs 5. Openness to Magick (10.2.1b, Type I) — Open to inspiration for this work 6. Cultivating Discipline (10.4.1) — Build lasting craft capacity 7. Commitment to Growth (10.4.2) — Establish lasting consistent practice 8. Discernment in Financial Matters (9.3.3b, Type I) — For launch decisions 9. Reception (8.3.2b, Type I) — Welcome support for this project

Note: Project-specific states (steps 1, 3, 5, 8, 9) use Type I—they serve THIS project and release when it's complete or established. Lasting capacities (steps 6-7) and financial clearing (step 2) use Type III.

12.5.4b Launching a Creative Project - Career Transformation

When the project IS the new career direction

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Deep, lasting purification 2. Clearing Financial Fear (9.1.1a, Type III) — Lasting clearing 3. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1a, Type III) — Lasting clarity about self as creator 4. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Clear limiting beliefs 5. Openness to Magick (10.2.1a, Type III) — Lasting creative openness 6. Cultivating Discipline (10.4.1) — Build lasting craft capacity 7. Commitment to Growth (10.4.2) — Establish lasting consistent practice 8. Discernment in Financial Matters (9.3.3a, Type III) — Lasting business discernment 9. Reception (8.3.2a, Type III) — Lasting receptivity to opportunity

Note: All Type III. This is identity-level transformation into a creative life.

12.5.5 Establishing New Relationship and Household

Moving in together, marriage, or partnership formation

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Both partners clear deeply 2. Releasing Past Relationships (11.2.3) — Complete old connections 3. Healing Past Relationship Wounds (11.1.4) — Heal relevant wounds 4. Honest Communication (11.4.1) — Establish clear communication 5. Deep Listening (11.4.2) — Build capacity to truly hear each other 6. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Create shared lasting space 7. Deepening Intimacy (11.5.1) — Deepen commitment 8. Financial Boundaries (9.5.2) — Protect shared resources 9. Growing Together (11.5.3b, Type III) — Establish sustainable growth patterns

Note: All Type III for lasting partnership installation. Step 9 uses Type III (not Type IV) to allow the relationship to evolve naturally. Upgrade to Type IV alternative (11.5.3a) only when certain of absolute permanent commitment.

12.5.6 Midlife Transformation

When fundamental reassessment is needed

1. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1a, Type III) — Face what's been avoided permanently 2. Shadow Integration (10.1.2a, Type III) — See lifelong patterns lastingly 3. Ego Right-Sizing (10.1.3) — Accept the full picture 4. Releasing Attachment Patterns (11.2.1b, Type I) — Release old expectations temporarily 5. Bond Breaking (8.5.1a, Type III) — If major severances needed 6. Integration (8.1.4) — Seal wounds 7. Breaking Self-Limiting Patterns (10.3.3) — Break limiting identities 8. Openness to Divine Knowledge (10.2.2a, Type III) — Embrace new possibilities lastingly 9. Cultivating Self-Love (11.1.1) — Love who you're becoming 10. Integration After Breakthrough (10.4.3) — Embody the new self

Note: Steps 1-2, 5, 8 use Type III for lasting identity-level shifts. Step 4 uses Type I—releasing old expectations is a processing phase that completes, not a permanent state. If midlife includes active search for new relationship, use 9.2.1a (Type III) instead.

12.5.7 Annual Renewal

Regular maintenance sequence for new year or personal anniversary

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Annual clearing 2. Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Call back scattered energy 3. Sanctuary Maintenance (8.2.2) — Refresh protections 4. Radical Self-Honesty (10.1.1b, Type I) — Annual honest assessment 5. Recognizing Opportunity (10.3.2b, Type I) — Clarify year's focus 6. Abundance Mindset Installation (9.2.1) — Renew positive orientation 7. Reception (8.3.2b, Type I) — Open to year's blessings

Note: Type I for steps 1, 4, 5, 7—annual renewal creates temporary heightened states for the new year's opening, not permanent installations. You'll renew again next year. Exception: if you've never done lasting versions, consider running the Type III alternatives first to establish permanent foundation, then use this Type I sequence for annual refresh.

12.5.8 Before Major Ritual or Ceremony

Preparation for important magical working — temporary heightened states

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1b, Type I) — Purification for this working 2. Sanctuary Purging (8.2.3b, Type I) — Clear working space for this ritual 3. Energy Reclamation (8.1.3) — Consolidate power 4. Openness to Magick (10.2.1b, Type I) — Open for this work 5. Discernment (10.3.1) — Ensure clear intention 6. Gatekeeping (8.3.1b, Type I) — Establish what may enter for this ritual 7. Reception (8.3.2b, Type I) — Open to beneficial forces for this working

Note: All Type I except step 5. Ritual preparation creates temporary heightened states that release after the working completes. You don't want permanent ritual-level purification or permanent gatekeeping—these serve THIS working. Step 5 uses Type III because lasting discernment serves all future workings.

12.5.9 Establishing Regular Magical Practice

For those beginning sustained magical work — lasting installations

1. Self-Cleansing (8.1.1a, Type III) — Deep, lasting purification 2. Sanctuary Establishment (8.2.1a, Type III) — Permanent working space 3. Openness to Magick (10.2.1a, Type III) — Lasting magical receptivity 4. Discernment (10.3.1) — Lasting discernment 5. Gatekeeping (8.3.1a, Type III) — Lasting boundary intelligence 6. Reception (8.3.2a, Type III) — Lasting beneficial reception 7. Cultivating Discipline (10.4.1) — Build practice capacity

Note: All Type III. This establishes permanent infrastructure for magical practice. Once installed, use Type I alternatives for individual ritual preparations (see "Before Major Ritual" above).

Part XIII: Quick Reference

Comprehensive reference materials for all system components and recipes.

13.1 System Fundamentals

Alchemical Colors

Black Dissolution, entropy, breakdown, shadow exposure, clearing White Purification, refinement, clarification, filtering, precision Green Generation, growth, organic expansion, connection, vitality Red Embodiment, manifestation, sovereignty, authority, completion Canonical Sequence: Black → White → Green → Red → Black...

Elemental Modes

Air Thought, communication, strategy, mental operations Water Emotion, intuition, receptivity, feeling operations Earth Stability, structure, grounding, building operations Fire Action, will, transformation, dynamic operations Canonical Sequence: Air → Water → Earth → Fire → Air...

Dyad Classes

Class 0 Identity (same color/element both positions) Maximum fixation, resistance to change Class +1 Progressive (forward in canonical sequence) Natural flow, developmental motion Class -1 Regressive (backward in canonical sequence) Return, withdrawal, reversal motion Class +/-2 Opposition (skip-level bridging) Dialectical tension, breakthrough potential

Configuration Types

Type I: Linear Transition (H ≠ I ≠ T, all different) Maximum flexibility, minimal self-maintenance Requires ongoing attention or naturally decays Easiest to reverse (often self-reverses) Type II: Origin Reinforcement (H = I, both differ from T) Momentum from starting point Moderate persistence, moderate reversal difficulty Working carries force of its origin Type III: Destination Locking (H = T, both differ from I) Self-maintaining at destination High persistence, requires active reversal Most common for lasting change Type IV: Absolute Identity (H = I = T, all same) Maximum permanence, sealed state Very difficult to reverse Use sparingly, only when permanence truly needed Type V: Parallel Reinforcement (I = T, both differ from H) Maintained constancy under external governance Used primarily in reversals Stable released state

• • •
